*  And they were not alone. [[02:24:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8677.9s)]
*  What might be called the riot ideology broadly took hold not only among many blacks, but among opinion and policymakers as well. [[02:24:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8679.9s)]
*  Post riot surveys showed that though whites and Latinos were resentful, [[02:24:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8687.9s)]
*  the riots boosted black self-esteem. [[02:24:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8692.9s)]
*  According to LA historian Rafael Sonenshine, [[02:24:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8694.9s)]
*  the riots unified, mobilized, and energized the black community politically. [[02:24:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8698.9s)]
*  Policymakers at the time didn't fully embrace the argument of radical sociologist Robert Blauner, [[02:25:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8704.9s)]
*  who insisted that the liberal humanist value that violence is the worst sin [[02:25:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8710.9s)]
*  cannot be defended today if one is committed squarely against racism and for self-determination. [[02:25:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8715.9s)]
*  But neither did they fully reject that, end quote. [[02:25:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8720.9s)]
*  The cities tried to cope and head off the crisis, [[02:25:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8726.9s)]
*  and the state and federal government tried to help them cope. [[02:25:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8730.9s)]
*  Lyndon Johnson's war on poverty can be looked at in retrospect [[02:25:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8734.9s)]
*  as an attempt by the federal government to take some of the burden of the great migration off the shoulders of local governments. [[02:25:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8739.9s)]
*  The big nonprofit foundations like the Ford Foundation, the Rockefeller Foundation, [[02:25:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8745.9s)]
*  all the outfits listed as sponsors whenever you listen to NPR, [[02:25:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8751.9s)]
*  had always in the past been focusing on things like building public libraries and setting up scholarship funds and jobs programs or [[02:25:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8755.9s)]
*  curing hookworm in the south. [[02:26:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8764.9s)]
*  But in the early days, the government was trying to do something about it. [[02:26:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8767.9s)]
*  In 1962, the Ford Foundation had created the Mobilization for Youth, [[02:26:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8770.9s)]
*  which received millions of dollars from the federal government to serve juvenile delinquents in Manhattan's Lower East Side. [[02:26:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8775.9s)]
*  The foundation was also involved in the creation of the Feds, [[02:26:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8783.9s)]
*  which had been the foundation for the first time in the last few decades. [[02:26:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8787.9s)]
*  The Feds were the foundation for the first time in the last few decades. [[02:26:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8792.9s)]
*  The Feds were the foundation for the first time in the last few decades. [[02:26:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8795.9s)]
*  Founded to provide opportunities for at-risk youth, [[02:26:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8801.9s)]
*  the Mobilization for Youth organization soon morphed into an early pioneer of the confrontation politics that would lead to the race riots later in the decade. [[02:26:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8805.9s)]
*  The Mobilization for Youth aimed to put into practice ideas about welfare reform [[02:26:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8815.9s)]
*  being promulgated by a group of radical left-wing sociologists at Columbia. [[02:27:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8821.9s)]
*  And I know that all of those descriptors are pretty redundant. [[02:27:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8827.9s)]
*  The sociologists would write openly back in the 60s about their goal [[02:27:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8831.9s)]
*  of bringing as many people as possible onto the welfare rolls with the explicit goal of overburdening state and local governments, [[02:27:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8837.9s)]
*  of ratcheting up racial and class tensions, [[02:27:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8846.9s)]
*  and of creating a powder keg that would blow past conservative resistance to more radical economic redistribution at the federal level. [[02:27:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8850.9s)]
*  That sounds like hyperbole. It gets even worse than that, though. [[02:27:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8858.9s)]
*  Two leading Columbia sociologists, Richard Cloward and Francis Fox Piven, [[02:27:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8862.9s)]
*  whose papers on welfare reform would soon be marching orders for the government of New York City, [[02:27:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8868.9s)]
*  wrote that, quote, When attachments to the role of work deteriorate, so do attachments to the family, especially the attachments of men to their families. [[02:27:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8873.9s)]
*  Well, that sounds like something a critic of welfare expansion would say, right? [[02:28:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8884.9s)]
*  They predicted that putting more people on welfare would lead to family breakdown and spread certain forms of disorder, [[02:28:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8890.9s)]
*  including school failure, crime, and addiction. [[02:28:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8899.9s)]
*  Well, these guys must really be against welfare expansion if they think it's going to lead to family breakdown, school failure, crime, and addiction, right? [[02:28:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8904.9s)]
*  In 1966, they elaborated that family breakdown would lead to a weakening of social control, especially over the young. [[02:28:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8914.9s)]
*  And it was the young who were the most prominent in the disorders of the 60s. [[02:28:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8923.9s)]
*  Sounds pretty bad and pretty prescient, right? [[02:28:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8928.9s)]
*  Here's the thing. These two were not dissident sociologists pushing back against the campaign to expand the welfare rules. [[02:28:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8932.9s)]
*  They were the most important and prominent advocates pushing for it. [[02:29:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8941.9s)]
*  They dismissed the politics of compromise and consensus as a bourgeois trick, [[02:29:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8946.9s)]
*  and they favored what they called dissensus politics. [[02:29:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8953.9s)]
*  Which was when a group or minority, quote, engages in actions which are designed to dislodge or threaten to dislodge [[02:29:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8956.9s)]
*  not only the minority, but more importantly, other significant constituent groups in that same alliance. [[02:29:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8965.9s)]
*  Through the cadre's ability to generate defections among other groups in a coalition, [[02:29:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8972.9s)]
*  its impact becomes far greater than the voting power of the minority. [[02:29:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8978.9s)]
*  If the strategists of consensus look for issues and actions to bring people in groups together, [[02:29:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8981.9s)]
*  then we strategists of dissensus look for issues and actions that will drive people apart, end quote. [[02:29:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8988.9s)]
*  Well, that's just a long-winded way of describing what revolutionaries everywhere had always referred to as agitation. [[02:29:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=8996.9s)]
*  These people believed that trying to help the poor, especially poor minorities, to lift themselves into the middle class [[02:30:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9002.9s)]
*  was at best a delaying tactic designed to mollify the poor with false illusions of progress and contain revolution. [[02:30:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9011.9s)]
*  Even those who were successful at getting into the middle class would have merely gone to the streets of the city [[02:30:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9022.9s)]
*  and started to get into the middle class, would have merely carved out their own place in an unequal, [[02:30:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9029.9s)]
*  hypocritical, and fundamentally racist society. [[02:30:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9036.9s)]
*  Effectively, they would have become collaborators with that society. [[02:30:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9041.9s)]
*  The system required total overhaul, not reform, revolution. [[02:30:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9046.9s)]
*  And the desperate poor with no attachments and nothing to lose were the best revolutionary foot soldiers welfare dollars could buy. [[02:30:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9053.9s)]
*  These people did not see the poor as potential members of the middle class. [[02:31:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9062.9s)]
*  That was a bad outcome as far as they were concerned. [[02:31:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9068.9s)]
*  They saw the poor and located the value of the poor in their potential as revolutionaries. [[02:31:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9071.9s)]
*  Fred Siegel writes, [[02:31:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9078.9s)]
*  The real power of the poor, argued Piven and Cloward, came from a street-smart version of self-help, their ability to menace and riot. [[02:31:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9081.9s)]
*  Rent strikes, crime, civic disruptions, they argued, are the politics of the poor. [[02:31:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9091.9s)]
*  In order to fend off the violence, or threat of violence, local government would have to open up the welfare rolls. [[02:31:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9097.9s)]
*  They assumed this would mean procedural turmoil in the cumbersome welfare bureaus and fiscal turmoil in the localities where existing sources of tax revenue were already overburdened. [[02:31:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9104.9s)]
*  The aim was to generate severe political strains and deepen existing divisions among elements in the big city democratic coalition, [[02:31:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9116.9s)]
*  the remaining white middle class, the white working class, ethnic groups, and the growing minority poor. [[02:32:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9126.9s)]
*  If the system could, through threat and intimidation, be overloaded, if New York City was faced with welfare bankruptcy, [[02:32:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9133.9s)]
*  then it was assumed the mayor and the governor would have to become lobbyists for change in Washington. [[02:32:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9142.9s)]
*  In 1966, New York City Mayor John Lindsay named Mitchell Ginsburg, [[02:32:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9150.9s)]
*  a board member of the Ford Foundation's Mobilization for Youth and a part of Cloward and Piven's clique at Columbia, [[02:32:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9160.9s)]
*  as his first commissioner of social services, and Mitchell got right to work, putting those ideas into practice. [[02:32:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9168.9s)]
*  He ordered his department to prepare an advertising campaign to encourage people to get on welfare, [[02:32:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9175.9s)]
*  and he mobilized other employees of his department and of the poverty agencies to go door to door trying to sign people up for benefits. [[02:33:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9182.9s)]
*  At the same time, he took dramatic steps to hobble his own agency's ability to properly vet people according to need. [[02:33:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9191.9s)]
*  He eliminated the interview and investigation process that was meant to see whether an applicant was really eligible, [[02:33:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9199.9s)]
*  and instead told the people at his agency that they were to rely solely on the applicant's word that they were eligible. [[02:33:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9207.9s)]
*  And so predictably, the welfare rolls absolutely exploded. [[02:33:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9214.9s)]
*  Meanwhile, the Mobilization for Youth hit the streets to do their part, staging sit-ins and riots at welfare offices. [[02:33:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9219.9s)]
*  And organizing Puerto Rican welfare mothers to have confrontations with employees of the welfare agency, [[02:33:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9229.9s)]
*  even leaving a load of dead rats on the doorstep of the mayor's residence. [[02:33:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9236.9s)]
*  Again, this is an organization conceived and funded by the Ford Foundation and federal government, [[02:34:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9241.9s)]
*  and one of its board members is serving as New York's welfare commissioner, and its employees are being paid to go out and create havoc. [[02:34:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9248.9s)]
*  The Mobilization for Youth was just one of countless organizations that received government and foundation funding to go raise hell on the streets. [[02:34:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9255.9s)]
*  Another one, the National Welfare Rights Association, or organization rather, NWRO, [[02:34:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9264.9s)]
*  strong-armed the New York City government by holding intense demonstrations in small riots and welfare offices, [[02:34:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9271.9s)]
*  and then bragged about how this strategy had forced the city to hand over $3 million in new grants to them over a five-week period. [[02:34:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9277.9s)]
*  By the late 60s, raising hell was a multi-billion dollar industry. [[02:34:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9285.9s)]
*  But the question was what to do with all this money. [[02:34:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9291.9s)]
*  City agencies tasked with distributing federal war on poverty funds had a problem. [[02:34:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9296.9s)]
*  Namely that their middle-class civil servants knew nothing at all about the impoverished ghettos where help was most needed. [[02:35:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9301.9s)]
*  So when word got out that the agencies had a pile of money that they didn't know what to do with, [[02:35:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9309.9s)]
*  enterprising locals in cities across the country set up organizations to help them figure it out. [[02:35:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9315.9s)]
*  In his essay, Maumauing the Flat Catchers, Tom Wolfe, a former mayor of New York City, [[02:35:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9321.9s)]
*  explains how the whole thing worked in humorous detail. [[02:35:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9327.9s)]
*  Starts off, quote, [[02:35:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9335.9s)]
*  Well, they used the ethnic catering service. [[02:35:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9357.9s)]
*  They sat back and waited for you to come rolling in with your certified angry militants, [[02:36:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9368.9s)]
*  your guaranteed frustrated ghetto youth looking like a bunch of wild men. [[02:36:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9374.9s)]
*  Then you had your test confrontation. [[02:36:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9379.9s)]
*  If you were outrageous enough, if you could shake up the bureaucrats so bad that their eyes froze into ice balls [[02:36:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9382.9s)]
*  and their mouths twisted up into smiles of sheer physical panic, into shit-eating grins, so to speak, [[02:36:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9389.9s)]
*  then they knew you were the real goods. [[02:36:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9396.9s)]
*  They knew you were the right studs to give the poverty grants and community organizing jobs to. [[02:36:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9399.9s)]
*  Otherwise, they wouldn't know. [[02:36:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9404.9s)]
*  Whites had been studying the urban Negro in every way they could think of for 15 years, [[02:36:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9406.9s)]
*  but they found out they didn't know any more about the ghettos than when they started. [[02:36:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9413.9s)]
*  Every time there was a riot, Whites would call on Negro leaders to try to cool it, [[02:36:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9417.9s)]
*  only to find out that the Negro leaders didn't have any followers. [[02:37:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9423.9s)]
*  They sent Martin Luther King into Chicago, and the people ignored him. [[02:37:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9427.9s)]
*  They sent Dick Gregory into Watts, and the people hooted at him and threw beer cans. [[02:37:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9431.9s)]
*  During the riot at Hunter's Point, the mayor of San Francisco, John Shelley, [[02:37:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9436.9s)]
*  went into Hunter's Point with the only black member of the board of supervisors, [[02:37:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9441.9s)]
*  and the brothers threw rocks at both of them. [[02:37:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9445.9s)]
*  They sent in the middle-class black members of the Human Rights Commission, [[02:37:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9448.9s)]
*  and the brothers laughed at them and called them Toms. [[02:37:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9452.9s)]
*  Then they figured that the leadership of the riots must be the gangs, [[02:37:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9455.9s)]
*  so they sent in the ex-gang leaders from groups like Youth for Service [[02:37:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9459.9s)]
*  to make a liaison with key gang leaders. [[02:37:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9464.9s)]
*  What they didn't know was that Hunter's Point and a lot of ghettos were so disorganized, [[02:37:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9468.9s)]
*  there weren't even any key gangs, much less key gang leaders in there. [[02:37:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9473.9s)]
*  That riot finally just burned itself out after five days, that was all. [[02:37:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9478.9s)]
*  But the idea that the real leadership in the ghetto might be the gangs [[02:38:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9483.9s)]
*  hung on with the poverty youth welfare establishment. [[02:38:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9486.9s)]
*  It was considered a very sophisticated insight. [[02:38:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9490.9s)]
*  The youth gangs weren't petty criminals, they were social bandits, primitive revolutionaries. [[02:38:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9493.9s)]
*  Of course, they were hidden from public view. [[02:38:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9500.9s)]
*  That was why the nature of ghetto leadership had eluded everyone for so long. [[02:38:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9503.9s)]
*  So the poverty professionals were always on the lookout for the bad acting dudes [[02:38:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9508.9s)]
*  who were the real leaders, the natural leaders, the charismatic figures in the ghetto jungle. [[02:38:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9512.9s)]
*  These were the kind of people the social welfare professionals in the Kennedy administration [[02:38:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9519.9s)]
*  had in mind when they planned the poverty program in the first place. [[02:38:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9524.9s)]
*  It was a truly adventurous and experimental approach they had. [[02:38:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9528.9s)]
*  Instead of handing out alms, which never seemed to change anything, [[02:38:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9532.9s)]
*  they would encourage people in the ghetto to organize. [[02:38:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9537.9s)]
*  They would help them become powerful enough to force the establishment to give them what they needed. [[02:38:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9539.9s)]
*  From the beginning, the poverty program was aimed at helping ghetto people rise up against their oppressors. [[02:39:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9546.9s)]
*  It was a scene in which the federal government came into the ghetto and said, [[02:39:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=9553.9s)]

*  and at least 40 percent of black kids lived in broken homes. [[02:50:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10245.9s)]

*  So as a result, the city government had no credibility or legitimacy with the people. [[02:50:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10254.9s)]
*  A few years after this time, a bunch of police and public officials would be indicted for being on the take from organized crime rings, [[02:51:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10260.9s)]
*  and no one was minding the store because the citizens who would have cared about the decline of the city, [[02:51:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10268.9s)]
*  they were not sticking around to try to stop it. They were just getting out. [[02:51:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10275.9s)]
*  Journalist Eugene Methven in his book The Riot Makers writes, [[02:51:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10279.9s)]
*  In 1964 and 65, Rutgers Center for Urban Studies took two polls of Newark Negro men, which revealed a volatile condition. [[02:51:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10285.9s)]
*  Almost a fifth of Newark's Negroes had sunk into enemy. [[02:51:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10297.9s)]
*  The label sociologist Emil Durkheim applied to a state of normlessness, disorganization, frustration, and bitterness, [[02:51:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10302.9s)]
*  in which people seek desired ends not by planning and rational action, but rather by spastic and pointless acts. [[02:51:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10311.9s)]
*  These Newark men were totally unorganized, unattached, amoral, and alienated. [[02:51:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10318.9s)]
*  They had no ties to churches, police, schools, or social workers. [[02:52:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10324.9s)]
*  They, quoting the Rutgers report, [[02:52:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10330.9s)]
*  Reject all forms of culturally sanctioned remedial agencies, including political parties, Negro action groups, legal personnel, and state agencies. [[02:52:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10333.9s)]
*  Instead, they had substituted a vague desire to fight back or a belief that the situation is hopeless. [[02:52:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10343.9s)]
*  In short, declared Leonard Zeitz, the sociologist who authored the report, [[02:52:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10351.9s)]
*  They hated everything. [[02:52:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10356.9s)]
*  Zeitz warned Newark City Hall, [[02:52:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10359.9s)]
*  The great danger present in this set of attitudes is that some force, as yet not evolved in the Negro community, [[02:52:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10361.9s)]
*  may come into being which may possibly crystallize the spastic hostility and formless apathy into a cohesive antagonistic force bent on self-destruction. [[02:52:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10369.9s)]
*  Well, SDS saw this as an opportunity, and so they began pouring into Newark. [[02:53:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10382.9s)]
*  SDS National Secretary Greg Calvert told a New York Times reporter, [[02:53:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10387.9s)]
*  We are working to build a guerrilla force in an urban environment. We are actively organizing sedition. [[02:53:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10393.9s)]
*  SDS got support from Communist Party USA, [[02:53:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10400.9s)]
*  Who sent Jesse Gray, their chief black organizer, who had helped precipitate a small riot in Harlem the year before. [[02:53:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10405.9s)]
*  During that riot, Gray had famously announced to a reporter that he was looking for [[02:53:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10413.9s)]
*  100 skilled black revolutionaries who were ready to die in guerrilla warfare. [[02:53:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10419.9s)]
*  SDS also got help from CORE, the Congress on Racial Equality, and other black militant groups. [[02:53:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10426.9s)]
*  So the activists rented a slum apartment and started off by knocking on doors to take surveys of people's grievances. [[02:53:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10434.9s)]
*  But this was really just a pretext to sound out the city's black residents and to find and recruit the people who were the most angry and the most ready to do something about it. [[02:54:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10441.9s)]
*  Soon they developed a cadre of local black residents and they put them to work agitating in their own neighborhoods, [[02:54:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10453.9s)]
*  organizing weekly meetings and working with CORE and other civil rights organizations to pull off protests and demonstrations of civil disobedience. [[02:54:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10460.9s)]
*  Not to call for any specific reforms or programs. This is very clear from their internal writings, just to turn up the temperature in the city. [[02:54:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10470.9s)]
*  Over time, they identified a handful of locals, maybe a hundred or so, who showed up for every meeting [[02:54:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10480.9s)]
*  and who would stand up to speak at rallies and who were the most vocal in their anger. [[02:54:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10488.9s)]
*  And they began developing them as an inner cadre that would plan more direct and dramatic action. [[02:54:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10493.9s)]
*  By summer 1965, SDS had been working to set conditions for nearly a year when President Johnson's war on poverty targeted Newark. [[02:55:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10501.9s)]
*  There was no better place for a war on poverty to target, but for the reasons I described earlier, [[02:55:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10513.9s)]
*  the way it was handled created more problems than it solved and sustained and exacerbated the ones it was supposed to fix. [[02:55:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10520.9s)]
*  Rather than spending the money themselves, local bureaucrats from the federal anti-poverty agencies would find local community organizations [[02:55:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10527.9s)]
*  who presumably knew the city and its population and their needs better than any bureaucrat and they just gave them the money to spend as they saw fit. [[02:55:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10537.9s)]
*  And so in Newark, civil rights leaders, mostly a bunch of ministers, moderate people, set up the United Community Corporation [[02:55:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10546.9s)]
*  to receive the millions of dollars that would be coming into the city and to put it to work. [[02:55:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10553.9s)]
*  The UCC divided Newark into eight districts called area boards, each of which got its cut of the money [[02:56:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10560.9s)]
*  and worked with independent authority over staff hiring and just how the money was spent in general. [[02:56:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10567.9s)]
*  Now when the war on poverty came to town, SDS, as I said, had already been on the ground getting organized for over a year, [[02:56:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10572.9s)]
*  so they were very ready to take advantage of it. [[02:56:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10580.9s)]
*  And so they began to agitate against the civil rights leaders who set up the United Community Corporation [[02:56:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10583.9s)]
*  and they put their activists to work telling the local black population that the program was a fraud [[02:56:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10589.9s)]
*  and that those black ministers are stealing or wasting the money and that new leadership was needed at the UCC. [[02:56:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10595.9s)]
*  The SDS leader on the ground in Newark, Tom Hayden, he bragged about how they got the community to protest against the program and its leaders. [[02:56:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10603.9s)]
*  He said, we tried the approach of implying that soon more city hall people would be paid to get rich, patrol, and rob. [[02:56:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10613.9s)]
*  We tried the approach of implying that soon more city hall people would be paid to get rich, patrol, and control the neighborhood [[02:57:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10620.9s)]
*  unless we did something to expose and resist them. [[02:57:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10627.9s)]
*  Well, it worked. Soon they got about 70 of their followers to take over a meeting of UCC area board number three, [[02:57:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10630.9s)]
*  which usually only had about 50 people show up, so their 70 just swamped it, [[02:57:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10641.9s)]
*  and they called for a vote on new leadership and got their own people elected as trustees and board chairmen. [[02:57:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10645.9s)]
*  Before long, they did the same with area board number two, which covered about 100,000 people in the city's central ward, [[02:57:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10652.9s)]
*  which was the black heartland of Newark. [[02:57:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10659.9s)]
*  Then they got strong footholds in area boards number five and seven, and in a very short period of time, [[02:57:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10662.9s)]
*  SDS, this organization whose national secretary is telling the New York Times that they are actively working to build a force for urban guerrilla warfare in America, [[02:57:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10667.9s)]
*  was running the war on poverty in Newark. [[02:57:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10678.9s)]
*  They had staff, they had offices, jobs to hand out, and millions of dollars from the federal government at their disposal. [[02:58:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10682.9s)]
*  SDS described its goals in one of its publications. [[02:58:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10691.9s)]
*  Success meant, this is a quote, success meant the project's ability to continually enlarge its diverse basis, [[02:58:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10695.9s)]
*  to penetrate all permeable local organizations and to create or control newly developing transitional structures, [[02:58:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10703.9s)]
*  while at the same time assuring its own autonomy, [[02:58:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10710.9s)]
*  so that its activity swings the level of the city's political dialogue and activity to the left. [[02:58:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10713.9s)]
*  As a locus of opposition in the city, the project's ability to create and control the city's political dialogue and activity to the left. [[02:58:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10719.9s)]
*  The project seeks to become associated with every manifestation of opposition activity. [[02:58:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10725.9s)]
*  The project must seek recruits and build opposition in whatever areas it can, and with whatever means present themselves. [[02:58:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10730.9s)]
*  In the course of its probing at all levels in the community, [[02:58:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10738.9s)]
*  the project also seeks to control or absorb established or new structures in the community that may become resources. [[02:59:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10741.9s)]
*  At every level, our goal is to disrupt, to challenge hollow democratic rhetoric, [[02:59:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10749.9s)]
*  to challenge authority, and to challenge the bases on which power is legitimated in society, end quote. [[02:59:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10755.9s)]
*  See, these people are not trying to help the black community of Newark. [[02:59:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10763.9s)]
*  They're trying to start a revolution. [[02:59:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10769.9s)]
*  They might tell themselves that after the revolution, the people of Newark, oh, they'll be much better off, [[02:59:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10772.9s)]
*  but in reality, that part of it never entered their minds. [[02:59:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10777.9s)]
*  That's not what they wrote about. That's not what they talked about. [[02:59:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10781.9s)]
*  It never entered their minds. The revolution was the thing. [[02:59:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10783.9s)]
*  Whatever came after could be dealt with after. [[02:59:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10787.9s)]
*  The Watts riot in 1965 opened their eyes to some new possibilities, [[02:59:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10791.9s)]
*  and they went to work to set conditions for a similar explosion in Newark. [[02:59:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10798.9s)]
*  That summer, a white cop shot a black suspect who had just knifed his partner, [[03:00:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10804.9s)]
*  and SDS saw the opportunity it needed. [[03:00:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10810.9s)]
*  Their mimeograph machines ran off thousands of flyers and leaflets denouncing and attacking the police. [[03:00:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10815.9s)]
*  They organized a march on City Hall, and they brought a truck with loudspeakers shouting slogans against the police. [[03:00:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10822.9s)]
*  They rounded up drunks and teenagers and put them in the crowd around City Hall, [[03:00:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10829.9s)]
*  while CORE ran their own marches and rallies at a downtown park. [[03:00:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10834.9s)]
*  Police began to find leaflets and flyers teaching people how to make Molotov cocktails [[03:00:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10839.9s)]
*  and to train them on overcoming police tactics during an uprising. [[03:00:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10846.9s)]
*  Caches of Molotov cocktails and other weapons were turned up by police in the Central Ward. [[03:00:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10850.9s)]
*  Firemen began to respond to false emergency calls [[03:00:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10856.9s)]
*  and went into booby-trapped buildings that were meant to maim them. [[03:01:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10861.9s)]
*  One of the battalion chiefs fell three stories when a stairwell that had been rigged to collapse under a grown man's weight fell out beneath him. [[03:01:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10866.9s)]
*  He ended up with a broken back. [[03:01:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10874.9s)]
*  In the first two years after SDS arrived in town, assaults on police officers more than doubled. [[03:01:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10877.9s)]
*  But even as the temperature turned up, the police department in Newark stood down [[03:01:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10886.9s)]
*  and totally failed to try to stem the growing unrest or to prepare for it when it eventually came. [[03:01:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10890.9s)]
*  The city's police director later told a New Jersey governor's commission that they had been afraid [[03:01:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10898.9s)]
*  that any actions they took would only provide more fodder for anti-police propaganda. [[03:01:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10904.9s)]
*  Well, the city did what it could to de-escalate the situation and respond to the people's demands. [[03:01:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10910.9s)]
*  The mayor was an Italian but a liberal Democrat and he integrated the city government. [[03:01:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10917.9s)]
*  He appointed black people to be his administrative assistant, his budget officer, the executive secretary of the city's planning board. [[03:02:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10924.9s)]
*  Newark had never had a black person sit on the city's zoning commission, so the mayor put a black person in charge of it. [[03:02:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10933.9s)]
*  He created a civil rights division in the city government. [[03:02:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10941.9s)]
*  He promoted black firemen and police officers to positions of higher authority. [[03:02:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10944.9s)]
*  The city got its first black chairman of education, its first black fire captain, its first black welfare director. [[03:02:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10950.9s)]
*  He instituted tough and real equal opportunity standards for city contracts. [[03:02:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10958.9s)]
*  And he stopped construction on a school after CORE complained about hiring discrimination with the construction companies. [[03:02:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10964.9s)]
*  He managed to squeeze the federal government for urban renewal grants, adding up to $286 per resident. [[03:02:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10970.9s)]
*  And with that money, the number of substandard housing units in the city was cut in half from 34% in 1960 to 16% by the summer of 67. [[03:02:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10978.9s)]
*  And so after the riots in other cities in 64, 65, and 66, [[03:03:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10990.9s)]
*  the Newark government breathed a sigh of relief, thinking that everything they were doing must be making a difference. [[03:03:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=10996.9s)]
*  They were wrong. [[03:03:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11004.9s)]
*  By 1967, SDS had set conditions in Newark, and they kicked off that year's protest season on April 1st by picketing a Jewish meat market they said was exploiting black people. [[03:03:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11007.9s)]
*  When that spring, the city raised a proposal to purchase property in the city's central slum and to move its residents into newly built projects some blocks away and use the area for a new state medical school, which would provide a lot of jobs had been had been approved already at the state level for Newark. [[03:03:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11017.9s)]
*  SDS had a proposal to move the city's property to the city's central slum. [[03:03:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11030.9s)]
*  When that spring, the city raised a proposal to purchase property in the city's central slum and to move its residents into newly built projects some blocks away and use the area for a new state medical school, which would provide a lot of jobs had been had been approved already at the state level for Newark. [[03:03:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11035.9s)]
*  SDS flyers on stationary bearing the name of one of the city's official anti poverty agencies said that the proposal was an attempt by whitey to use Negro removal to maintain their power in the city. [[03:04:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11050.9s)]
*  The city was keenly turned into raucous demonstrations near riots with SDS and their local activists doing everything they could to just shut the meetings down. [[03:04:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11065.9s)]
*  One leader told the board that blood would flow in the streets if the medical school project went forward. [[03:04:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11075.9s)]
*  Methan writes, quote, The catalytic figure was one Hassan Jeru Ahmed, a flamboyant 42 year old wig salesman and self commissioned Colonel from Washington, D.C. [[03:04:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11083.9s)]
*  Hassan had a police record, including arrests in 1966 for passing 21 worthless checks in Washington, D.C., a 1957 forgery sentence of two years in Pittsburgh, and a 1950 commitment for mental observation. [[03:04:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11096.9s)]
*  With a couple of lieutenants, Colonel Hassan showed up in Newark in late March on the invitation of SDS leaders in the city. [[03:05:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11112.9s)]
*  Sporting bizarre uniforms, black berets and fezzes, Hassan and company opened a black liberation center in a central ward storefront, hung out a photo of Malcolm X and a banner proclaiming the Black Panther is coming, and hooked up a loud speaker to broadcast to passersby. [[03:05:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11120.9s)]
*  They immediately linked up with SDSers from area board number three, whose president endorsed the new operation. [[03:05:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11138.9s)]
*  Soon neighbors reported to police that unidentified Negroes were conducting rifle target practice behind Hassan's center. [[03:05:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11146.9s)]
*  At his first rally on April 20th, Colonel Hassan told his listeners that the government was preparing army bases for use as concentration camps for Negroes. [[03:05:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11154.9s)]
*  His literature accused whites of playing the final trickery upon black men before opening the gates of all-out genocidal slaughter. [[03:06:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11164.9s)]
*  Hassan mixed violent words with violent action and brought Negro residents flocking to the city hall hearings on the medical school just to see his pyrotechnics. [[03:06:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11174.9s)]
*  One Sunday afternoon, May 21st, Hassan held a We Ain't Gonna Move rally to set the stage for the first medical school site hearing the next day. [[03:06:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11184.9s)]
*  Speakers included the defeated Negro candidate for mayor, the leader of the local corps branch, and one other Negro politician who urged the crowd, [[03:06:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11195.9s)]
*  If you expect to get anything for yourselves, you will have to give and take some physical beatings. [[03:06:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11205.9s)]
*  Hassan, proclaiming that even a small number of people could create a disruptive demonstration, led a rehearsal. [[03:06:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11211.9s)]
*  He had his audience rhythmically yell the word, No, louder and louder until the whole building shook. [[03:06:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11219.9s)]
*  Even the small group there, he declared, could start destroying the white man's precious property and force whitey to want to stop and talk it over. [[03:07:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11225.9s)]
*  Hassan announced, and the news media widely publicized, that the next day he would lead a large group, a battalion of 250 black beret mercenaries, from his black man's liberation army, to the hearing. [[03:07:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11235.9s)]
*  We'll tear the joint down if we have to. We expect trouble with the police, and we're counting on there being at least 100 policemen there to stop us, he proclaimed. [[03:07:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11249.9s)]
*  Within minutes after the city hall hearing opened, the wife of a Hassan lieutenant hurled eggs at board members on the dais. [[03:07:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11259.9s)]
*  Either trying to duck or stop the throwing, a reporter in the front row tangled with the woman, and her husband slugged him. [[03:07:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11267.9s)]
*  Police carted the struggling couple out. The audience clapped and stomped periodically as Hassan and other militants delivered fiery speeches. [[03:07:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11274.9s)]
*  Hassan led the audience in heaping insults on the Negro chairman of the committee, calling him a tom and a house nigger. [[03:08:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11282.9s)]
*  Raising slum buildings on the medical school site was a political move to get rid of Negro votes, Hassan cried. [[03:08:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11290.9s)]
*  He climaxed his pyrotechnics by leaping across the room, ripping up the stenographer's transcript, and hurling his machine against the wall. [[03:08:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11297.9s)]
*  At that, police carried him out, struggling, amid screams from the crowd. [[03:08:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11306.9s)]
*  Then another lieutenant, Captain Raffio, hurled a map rack at the board members on the dais. [[03:08:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11311.9s)]
*  The hearing dissolved in a general melee. [[03:08:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11317.9s)]
*  Incredibly, Newark officials decided that neither Hassan nor his lieutenants should be prosecuted. They were simply released. [[03:08:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11320.9s)]
*  Here was an open signal for all to see. City Hall no longer had the moral nerve to enforce law and order in Newark in the face of violent challenge. [[03:08:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11329.9s)]
*  This went on for months. [[03:09:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11342.9s)]
*  Hassan took his crew to a board of education meeting that devolved into a melee and had to be shut down. [[03:09:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11345.9s)]
*  He met with a group of radical black elementary school teachers and got them to hand out leaflets to their kids to give to their parents that read, [[03:09:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11352.9s)]
*  Are your kids getting kicked around? Your black children are being cheated out of their education. [[03:09:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11361.9s)]
*  Are you sick of white people running black schools? Come to the board of education meeting. [[03:09:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11367.9s)]
*  Another leaflet read, [[03:09:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11373.9s)]
*  Black men and black women, now is the time to unite in a solid front in the black revolution. [[03:09:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11374.9s)]
*  We are fed up with tyrants who lie, steal, and cheat our people. [[03:09:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11381.9s)]
*  Defeat the white race. Do not sit idly by. [[03:09:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11386.9s)]
*  More leaflets with instructions for making bombs and Molotov cocktails, [[03:09:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11390.9s)]
*  and for how to most effectively torch a building and what to say to police if arrested during a riot were papered all over the city. [[03:09:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11395.9s)]
*  Young school children were paid to post and distribute these leaflets all over their neighborhoods. [[03:10:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11404.9s)]
*  The city complained to the Federal Anti-Poverty Agency that the funds they were sending were going to radical groups trying to foment unrest. [[03:10:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11411.9s)]
*  The city said, [[03:10:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11421.9s)]
*  The acceleration of this kind of practice by the Anti-Poverty Agency will undoubtedly lead to riots and anarchy in our city. [[03:10:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11423.9s)]
*  Well, by mid-June, militants were turning virtually every city meeting open to the public into a near riot, [[03:10:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11431.9s)]
*  as more activists from SDS, CORE, and the Communist Party in New York poured into Newark to add their bit of fuel to the fire. [[03:10:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11440.9s)]
*  The radical black playwright, Leroy Jones, about whom we will have more to say later, [[03:10:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11449.9s)]
*  shouted at one city committee hearing, [[03:10:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11456.9s)]
*  At that meeting, the angry crowd screamed and threatened the committee all night long, [[03:10:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11459.9s)]
*  and the committee tried to wait them out, but at 3.30 a.m. they decided to adjourn until the next evening, [[03:11:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11473.9s)]
*  at which point the protesters took over the hearing room and declared that the city government's board was no longer in effect and that a new people's board had replaced the committee. [[03:11:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11479.9s)]
*  Well, by July, everybody knew what was coming. It was just a question of when. [[03:11:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11492.9s)]
*  The police department was begging the state and other localities for riot gear, [[03:11:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11498.9s)]
*  and the head of the New Jersey Fraternal Order of Police said that the city was as keyed up as an armed camp awaiting an attack. [[03:11:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11504.9s)]
*  On July 13, 1967, the attack was launched. [[03:11:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11512.9s)]
*  Two Newark patrol cops were cruising the city when a taxi started tailgating them, [[03:11:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11518.9s)]
*  revving up his engine behind them at a stoplight and flicking his headlights at them. [[03:12:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11524.9s)]
*  And so they got behind the cab and pulled it over, but before they could say license and registration, [[03:12:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11529.9s)]
*  the black driver shouted, What the fuck you call this, you white motherfuckers? [[03:12:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11535.9s)]
*  And so they ordered him to step out of the car, and as he got out, [[03:12:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11539.9s)]
*  he threw a haymaker sucker punch at one of the cops and busted up his mount. [[03:12:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11543.9s)]
*  And so the other officer tackles him while his partner recovers, and the two cops subdued him and arrested the man. [[03:12:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11548.9s)]
*  Very soon word began to circulate that a black man had been violently arrested by white cops, and the SDS cadre sprang into action. [[03:12:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11557.9s)]
*  The area board number three chairman ordered all the poverty workers on his payroll to go to the fourth precinct ready for action, [[03:12:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11566.9s)]
*  and he began putting in phone calls for reinforcements. [[03:12:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11574.9s)]
*  Protesters gathered outside the station house, and a few of the protest leaders were allowed inside to go see and talk to the man who was arrested, [[03:12:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11578.9s)]
*  who was then taken to a hospital with a cracked rib and a lump on the back of his head. [[03:13:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11588.9s)]
*  But the crowd outside was not in a mood to be placated, and they started throwing rocks and bricks at the police station. [[03:13:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11591.9s)]
*  The city's police director arrived on scene only to be hospitalized by rocks thrown from the roof of the 14 story housing project across the street. [[03:13:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11599.9s)]
*  And then around midnight, a fire bomb exploded, and then a car was torched in the parking lot across the street. [[03:13:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11609.9s)]
*  When firemen tried to deal with it, they were attacked by a mob, and then another car was on fire. [[03:13:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11616.9s)]
*  And so the police decided they should go out and disperse the crowd, and so they tried. [[03:13:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11623.9s)]
*  And the crowd scattered, but this just spread the chaos into a wider area. [[03:13:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11628.9s)]
*  A block away, a garbage can was thrown to the window of a liquor store and then other nearby businesses, and they were all looted. [[03:13:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11633.9s)]
*  The police managed to get the situation under control and only had to make 11 arrests that night. [[03:14:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11640.9s)]
*  By 2.30 a.m., the crowd had gone home to sleep it off. [[03:14:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11646.9s)]
*  The Newark News headline the next day read, Mayor's Appraisal, Trouble in Central Ward, Called an Isolated Incident. [[03:14:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11651.9s)]
*  But nobody really thought about it. [[03:14:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11661.9s)]
*  Around noon the next day, a gas station attendant saw that the 90 car parking lot of the housing project across the street from the station was completely empty, and he had never seen it anything but completely full. [[03:14:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11663.9s)]
*  Everybody in those apartments knew there was going to be a riot, and they didn't want their own car in the war zone. [[03:14:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11676.9s)]
*  That morning, SDS activists were distributing leaflets telling people to come to a mass rally at the 4th Precinct that afternoon. [[03:14:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11682.9s)]
*  But somehow the Newark police didn't catch wind of it, so they were caught off guard when people started showing up. [[03:14:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11689.9s)]
*  Hundreds of people came at the appointed time. [[03:14:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11695.9s)]
*  The police were called in and they were told to leave the building. [[03:14:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11699.9s)]
*  James Thret, the African American director of the city's Human Rights Commission, showed up to try to calm things down. [[03:15:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11702.9s)]
*  Lifted up on the shoulders of two men to get above the crowd, he announced that [[03:15:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11710.9s)]
*  the mayor is going to appoint a Negro captain in the police department. [[03:15:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11715.9s)]
*  You're going to have the first of your men be the captain of the police department. [[03:15:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11719.9s)]
*  The crowd just screamed that he was an Uncle Tom. [[03:15:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11722.9s)]
*  Later on he said, [[03:15:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11726.9s)]
*  I did not sense it until I was lifted up where I could look down into their eyes. [[03:15:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11728.9s)]
*  And then I knew I was in a mob. [[03:15:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11733.9s)]
*  They called me Tom and house nigger and such. [[03:15:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11736.9s)]
*  They were laughing on the outside, but I was still in the middle of the night. [[03:15:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11739.9s)]
*  I was still in the middle of the night. [[03:15:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11743.9s)]
*  I was still in the middle of the night. [[03:15:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11746.9s)]
*  They called me Tom and house nigger and such. [[03:15:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11748.9s)]
*  They were laughing on the outside and crying with hate on the inside. [[03:15:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11751.9s)]
*  Even the blackness of my face did not keep me from being a part of the man. [[03:15:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11755.9s)]
*  And I knew it was time to go. [[03:16:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11760.9s)]
*  And so he turned toward the door of the police station and as he headed in, a bottle smashed against his heels. [[03:16:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11765.9s)]
*  And as if it had been a signal, the crowd began hurling all manner of missiles at the station house. [[03:16:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11771.9s)]
*  Shattering windows and sending people inside scrambling for cover. [[03:16:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11776.9s)]
*  And this went on for two hours. [[03:16:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11781.9s)]
*  As police just hid inside, putting up benches and tables against windows and doors. [[03:16:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11784.9s)]
*  Protesters left and came back with loads of bricks and bottles and rocks and cinder blocks to throw at the building. [[03:16:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11792.9s)]
*  A squad of officers was dispatched out the back door to try to surprise and flank the crowd and try to chase them away. [[03:16:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11801.9s)]
*  But within minutes, they streamed back in wounded and bleeding. [[03:16:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11809.9s)]
*  Methven writes, quote, About 915 p.m., four officers in an unmarked police car, all its windows smashed, picked up fourth precinct captain Charles Zizza at his home. [[03:16:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11813.9s)]
*  About 930, they pulled onto the Newark Ghetto's main drag, Springfield Avenue. [[03:17:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11825.9s)]
*  Zizza gasped. Before them was an incredible carnival of piracy. [[03:17:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11831.9s)]
*  And now quoting the captain, We just saw masses of people. [[03:17:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11836.9s)]
*  Must have been 10,000 over 10 blocks. [[03:17:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11840.9s)]
*  Men, women and children smashing windows, looting, singing, shouting, setting fires. [[03:17:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11843.9s)]
*  The only vehicles in sight were about six cars and pickups with heavy chains hooked to the rear. [[03:17:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11849.9s)]
*  Men were heaving these chains over the steel grills and bars in front of store windows and snatching them right out. [[03:17:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11855.9s)]
*  And as far as we could see, there was not a single police car or policeman in sight. [[03:17:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11861.9s)]
*  And now back to Methven. [[03:17:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11866.9s)]
*  At Seventh Street, Zizza saw four men smashing the windows of a ladies apparel store. [[03:17:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11868.9s)]
*  It was too much for him. A lifelong cop. [[03:17:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11873.9s)]
*  Stop the car, he barked and with a bound was out, leading his four officers. [[03:17:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11875.9s)]
*  The four looters were in the store windows, undressing mannequins. [[03:18:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11881.9s)]
*  Zizza collared one, cowed another with his pistol and fired a fast shot at a third who fled around the corner. [[03:18:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11885.9s)]
*  This was the first shot and the first arrest of a looter in the Newark riot. [[03:18:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11892.9s)]
*  It was also the first attempt by the Newark Police Department in well over two hours of wholesale rioting to enforce the law. [[03:18:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11897.9s)]
*  On Springfield Avenue. [[03:18:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11905.9s)]
*  Zizza and his crew put three prisoners in their car, firing a shot or two in the air to hold snarling packs of rioters at bay. [[03:18:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11907.9s)]
*  At the fourth precinct, they found chaos, senior officers and foot patrolmen in unbelievable disarray. [[03:18:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11916.9s)]
*  Zizza's first words were, what the fuck are all these cops doing in here? Why aren't they out on the street? [[03:18:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11923.9s)]
*  It took urgent minutes to get any semblance of organization restored. [[03:18:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11929.9s)]
*  But within an hour, Zizza, a man with the veteran military commander's habit of command, took a dozen shotgun armed officers up on Springfield Avenue and marched them in a picket line down the street, driving looters before them without firing a shot. [[03:18:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11934.9s)]
*  The first bad fire, a children's furniture store, was already an inferno. [[03:19:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11949.9s)]
*  Zizza called for a radio equipped emergency truck and soon had a mobile command post in the Springfield riot area. [[03:19:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11954.9s)]
*  By midnight, they had cleared a good part of the avenue, made several arrests and begun receiving sniper fire from the rooftops. [[03:19:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11962.9s)]
*  As fast as police cleared looters out along Springfield, they simply shifted to other sections. [[03:19:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11970.9s)]
*  In the South Ward, a mob led by an ex-pugilist and bouncer in a local bar looted a Sears Roebuck store of 24 rifles. [[03:19:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11976.9s)]
*  In a demonstration of the rioters' pre-planning and organization, fire hydrants throughout the riot zone had been opened up to spray into the street in order to take away the water pressure firefighters needed to extinguish fires. [[03:19:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=11988.9s)]
*  The snipers seemed to multiply, and police officers and white civilians who were stupid enough to go outside came under fire from rooftops and windows. [[03:20:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12006.9s)]
*  Around 2.30 a.m., a message came over the police radio. A green Volkswagen bus with three black men inside was heading west on Springfield Avenue, shooting at targets as they passed by. [[03:20:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12017.9s)]
*  When the police located and stopped the van, the men didn't shoot at the cops, and inside the van was the playwright, Leroy Jones, and two workers from the poverty program in town. [[03:20:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12031.9s)]
*  The looting went on all night long, and at 4.10 a.m., the first rioter was killed by a policeman. [[03:20:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12044.9s)]
*  The next morning, the state governor came to Newark to assess the damage. [[03:20:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12053.9s)]
*  He saw people lined up in front of smash stores, some of them driving grocery carts, just casually looting every business in the area. [[03:20:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12057.9s)]
*  He saw a black couple stop their brand new Cadillac in the middle of the street, go into a shoe store, and loot everything they could carry. [[03:21:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12069.9s)]
*  The rioters were having a great time. The governor told a newsman that the whole thing had a holiday atmosphere. [[03:21:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12078.9s)]
*  The National Guard began trooping into the city the next day. [[03:21:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12084.9s)]
*  The riot zone was cordoned off as officials bickered over a plan of action, and even with the National Guard in town, the looting and burning continued throughout the day. [[03:21:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12088.9s)]
*  A black Muslim calling himself Haking X told a Life magazine reporter that the riots would continue until every white man's building in Newark is burned. [[03:21:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12098.9s)]
*  They didn't get all of them, but in the end, over a thousand businesses were looted and many of them burned. [[03:21:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12108.9s)]
*  At 5.10 p.m. on Friday, a police officer was killed by sniper fire from an upper floor window of the Scudder Homes housing project. [[03:21:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12116.9s)]
*  The police who were there on scene lost their minds and responded with wild gunfire and gunfire. [[03:22:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12127.9s)]
*  The police who were there on scene lost their minds and responded with wild gunfire and ended up killing a 74-year-old innocent bystander and wounding several others. [[03:22:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12134.9s)]
*  Word of a slain officer spread around the department, and panicky cops began shooting at anything that looked like a threat. [[03:22:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12144.9s)]
*  National Guardsmen and State Police and the Newark Police wound up shooting at each other on several occasions. [[03:22:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12153.9s)]
*  Now these snipers were not just random shooters. These were squads of riflemen who had been trained for the purpose. [[03:22:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12160.9s)]
*  They moved to a different floor after taking each shot. They moved from building to building around the riot zone. [[03:22:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12169.9s)]
*  Gradually the police and the guard managed to get things under control. [[03:22:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12177.9s)]
*  Mostly it was just that the rioters gave up out of exhaustion after several days and nights of non-stop carnage. [[03:23:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12182.9s)]
*  An amateur writer named Jules Spohn, who had been born in Newark in 1941 and lived there his entire life, wrote, [[03:23:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12188.9s)]
*  According to Russell Sackett, a reporter with Life magazine, reporters had a clandestine meeting with members of the sniper organizations near the outskirts of the riot zone. [[03:23:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12200.9s)]
*  The Newark snipers belonged to a group of young civil rights workers that was formed in Mississippi back in 1965. [[03:23:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12212.9s)]
*  The group had fraternal contact with other black extremist organizations such as RAM, the Revolutionary Action Movement, [[03:23:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12220.9s)]
*  US, the Swahili-speaking group in Los Angeles, and the Deacons for Defense and Justice. [[03:23:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12228.9s)]
*  He was told there were more than 50 members of this group who were active in and around Newark. [[03:23:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12235.9s)]
*  Members of the Black Nationalist, Black Muslim, Black Panther, and other insurrectionist groups were already in this city stirring up trouble. [[03:24:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12241.9s)]
*  Many of these insurrectionists came from California, Pennsylvania, New York, Ohio, and other states. [[03:24:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12250.9s)]

*  The Black community knew well in advance that these armed agitators were in the city and did nothing to stop them and actually aided and abetted them. [[03:24:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12264.9s)]
*  Of the 1,381 Negroes arrested, only 662 had prior criminal records. [[03:24:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12273.9s)]

[[03:26:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12361.9s)]
*  Businesses in the downtown area were finding it harder and harder to get people to come to work downtown for fear, real fear, of being mugged and held up on the way to or coming home from work. [[03:26:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=12376.9s)]

*  then the government has to do all those things. [[04:19:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15572.9s)]
*  And it's like Charlie LaDuff said, [[04:19:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15575.9s)]
*  negative changes hit the ghetto first, the trailer park second, [[04:19:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15578.9s)]
*  and then finally start working their way up into the middle class. [[04:19:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15582.9s)]
*  And that is what we have been seeing since the 1960s. [[04:19:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15585.9s)]
*  The decimation of families and communities created a terrible situation for inner-city blacks first, [[04:19:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15589.9s)]
*  but eventually those same trends caught up with poor whites and then working class whites. [[04:19:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15597.9s)]
*  And Charles Murray shows in his book, Coming Apart, [[04:20:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15601.9s)]
*  the statistics clearly demonstrate that poor and working class whites have been on the same downward trajectory [[04:20:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15604.9s)]
*  already traveled by poor and working class blacks in decades past. [[04:20:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15611.9s)]
*  So anyway, that was a long aside. [[04:20:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15617.9s)]
*  In the aftermath of the 67 riots, [[04:20:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15622.9s)]
*  President Lyndon Johnson set up the National Advisory Committee on Civil Disturbances, [[04:20:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15625.9s)]
*  better known as the Kerner Commission, [[04:20:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15631.9s)]
*  to study the causes of the rise in urban violence. [[04:20:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15634.9s)]
*  And since New York City was the most notable big city to have avoided major rioting, [[04:20:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15637.9s)]
*  the city's mayor, John Lindsay, was asked to lead the Kerner Commission. [[04:20:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15642.9s)]
*  Now John Lindsay was the quintessential leader of the 67 riots. [[04:20:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15648.9s)]
*  Eastern establishment, Rockefeller Republican. [[04:20:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15655.9s)]
*  A Yale-educated, elite liberal, enlightened on racial questions, [[04:20:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15659.9s)]
*  and seething with contempt for the ethnic groups and ethnic politics [[04:21:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15667.9s)]
*  that had shaped city life in the East and Midwest for over a century. [[04:21:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15674.9s)]
*  For Lindsay, the protests of an Italian or Lithuanian or Polish community [[04:21:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15677.9s)]
*  against the relocation of a public housing project to their neighborhood [[04:21:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15683.9s)]
*  had no more legitimacy than the wails of white Southerners who didn't want to share a drinking fountain. [[04:21:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15688.9s)]
*  They were the same thing as far as he was concerned. [[04:21:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15694.9s)]
*  In the Kerner report that eventually came out reflected that perspective. [[04:21:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15697.9s)]
*  It concluded that the causes of urban violence were not just the violence of the city, [[04:21:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15702.9s)]
*  but the causes of urban violence were economic inequality, failed social services, [[04:21:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15707.9s)]
*  police brutality, and media bias, all of which existed and continue to exist [[04:21:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15713.9s)]
*  because of the racism latent or active in the hearts of white Americans. [[04:21:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15718.9s)]
*  Not white Americans like him, of course. [[04:22:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15724.9s)]
*  Well, when Lindsay's attention turned to the schools, Lindsay asked the Ford Foundation, [[04:22:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15728.9s)]
*  who have already caused enough trouble in this episode, [[04:22:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15734.9s)]
