*  Bundy's tenure at the Ford Foundation was defined by its focus on racial issues. [[04:22:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15765.9s)]
*  When they weren't funding urban decay, like I described earlier, [[04:22:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15772.9s)]
*  outfits like the Ford Foundation were studying it, [[04:22:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15777.9s)]
*  and that's what Mayor Lindsay had tapped McGeorge Bundy to do for New York schools. [[04:23:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15780.9s)]
*  The New York public school system by this time served about 1.1 million students. [[04:23:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15784.9s)]
*  It employed 70,000 teachers, 43,000 administrators, [[04:23:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15792.9s)]
*  and it was and still is the largest school system in the country. [[04:23:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15799.9s)]
*  When the Brown v. Board of Education Supreme Court ruling to desegregate the southern schools was handed down in 1954, [[04:23:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15803.9s)]
*  New York City activists and education bureaucrats sprang into action. [[04:23:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15812.9s)]
*  At the time, the ruling was understood by most Americans outside the South [[04:23:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15817.9s)]
*  as something intended to strike a blow against Jim Crow in the South. [[04:23:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15824.9s)]
*  And they were right about that, but they were wrong that that's what it was only about. [[04:23:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15829.9s)]
*  Because almost as soon as the ink was dry on the ruling, [[04:23:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15835.9s)]
*  people were on the clock looking for ways to make it apply to institutions other than schools, [[04:24:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15840.9s)]
*  and not just in the South, but everywhere. [[04:24:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15844.9s)]
*  In the ruling, the court had overruled previous decisions, [[04:24:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15848.9s)]
*  which had permitted segregation as long as everyone had access to institutions and facilities of the same general quality. [[04:24:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15854.9s)]
*  It's called separate but equal is the way they put it. [[04:24:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15862.9s)]
*  In the Brown ruling, the court said that it was impossible for separate but equal to exist, [[04:24:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15865.9s)]
*  because under segregation, even if the segregated facility had the same quality as everywhere else across the board in every measurable way, [[04:24:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15870.9s)]
*  it still wouldn't be equal because the very act of segregating some people inevitably generated, according to the court, [[04:24:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15880.9s)]
*  quote, a feeling of inferiority as to their status in the community that may affect their hearts and minds in a way unlikely to ever be undone, end quote. [[04:24:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15889.9s)]
*  So proponents of integration argued for a very broad reading of this ruling. [[04:24:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15899.9s)]
*  They said that since the spirit of the court's decision was that any segregated institution or facility did unlawful violence to the psyche of the minorities they served, [[04:25:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15907.9s)]
*  then it didn't matter whether the segregation was accomplished legally as it had been in the South [[04:25:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15919.9s)]
*  or just naturally by people sorting themselves into different neighborhoods as it did in the North. [[04:25:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15925.9s)]
*  Diane Ravitch, the historian of New York's public school system, writes, quote, [[04:25:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15931.9s)]
*  Militant integrationists in the North, anxious to erase the stigma of racism that had permeated American society from its beginnings, [[04:25:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15937.9s)]
*  read the decision to mean that any large clustering of Blacks was evidence of racism. [[04:25:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15946.9s)]
*  From this perspective came the proposition that democratic ideals require the dispersion of Blacks in equal proportions [[04:25:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15953.9s)]
*  and always in a minority throughout the New York City school system. [[04:26:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15961.9s)]
*  The assumption was made and stated openly by leaders of the integration movement and by school officials in both city and state [[04:26:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15964.9s)]
*  that a school where Blacks predominated was by definition incapable of providing equal educational opportunity. [[04:26:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15972.9s)]
*  No matter what kinds of teachers or facilities or pupils a school had, [[04:26:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15980.9s)]
*  even a school in which every pupil was the intellectual equivalent of Frederick Douglass or Stokely Carmichael or Roy Wilkins, [[04:26:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15985.9s)]
*  a Black school could never be a good school in the eyes of militant integrationists. [[04:26:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15992.9s)]
*  Thus, the effort to eliminate all forms of racism, whether written or unwritten, [[04:26:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=15998.9s)]
*  turned into a well-intentioned but ill-fated demand that no school have an enrollment that was more than 50% Black or 50% Black in Puerto Rican. End quote. [[04:26:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16004.9s)]
*  Well, the problem was that with so much rapid demographic transformation, integration became a moving target. [[04:26:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16015.9s)]
*  During the 1950s, New York City lost over 800,000 mostly middle-class White residents [[04:27:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16024.9s)]
*  and gained over 700,000 mostly poor Black and Puerto Rican residents. [[04:27:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16033.9s)]
*  Schools which, as recently as 1955 or even 1960, had been considered integrated became by the mid-60s almost entirely Black and Puerto Rican. [[04:27:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16038.9s)]
*  Well, to counter this self-segregation taking place, the city started an open enrollment program to allow Black students to participate in the school. [[04:27:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16050.9s)]
*  And so, with this self-segregation taking place, the city started an open enrollment program to allow students in Black neighborhoods to transfer to middle-class White schools in other parts of town. [[04:27:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16061.9s)]
*  It was a voluntary program. And transportation was paid for by the city. [[04:27:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16074.9s)]
*  Teachers and principals in the inner city were against the program because they thought that all that it would do, and I can understand where they're coming from, [[04:27:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16079.9s)]
*  was take away their best students, the ones with enough interest in school and concern from parents to actually take advantage of the program. [[04:28:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16086.9s)]
*  And so the student population left behind would be in even worse shape than it was currently. [[04:28:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16095.9s)]
*  And Black parents and students were not enthusiastic about the program either. [[04:28:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16101.9s)]
*  Despite the insistence of Black activists, the reality was that neither kids nor parents were really excited about being bussed halfway across the city to attend an unfamiliar school. [[04:28:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16106.9s)]
*  A lot of single mothers had to work, and they couldn't be around to make sure that their kid made it back from some faraway school in another borough. [[04:28:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16119.9s)]
*  And so as a result, only about 677 students, I guess that's not an about, that's pretty precise, only 677 students total took advantage of the program. [[04:28:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16129.9s)]
*  No government program could overcome the demographic reality. [[04:29:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16143.9s)]
*  While the overall number of K-12 students in New York City public schools dropped by 8% between 1956 and 1963, the number of Black students grew by 53% in those same years. [[04:29:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16149.9s)]
*  By the end of that period, Black and Puerto Rican kids made up a straight majority of all students in the public schools. [[04:29:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16167.9s)]
*  So even if every student in the city was spread out evenly across the whole system, the minority kids would just make up 53% of every school instead of 90% of some of the schools. [[04:29:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16175.9s)]
*  Whole swaths of the city and the surrounding areas, big, big areas were now overwhelmingly Black. [[04:29:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16189.9s)]
*  And so to even move in the direction of integration would have meant busing Black kids, again, halfway across the city to go to school in white areas, and forcing parents in those white areas to have their kids bused halfway across the city into the ghetto. [[04:29:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16196.9s)]
*  That was a political non-starter, obviously. [[04:30:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16211.9s)]
*  The way it was put by the chairman of the city's Board of Education was, the schools cannot solve a problem created by the residential decisions of the people of New York. [[04:30:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16214.9s)]
*  We would think that having a total city student population that was 53% Black and Puerto Rican would be a pretty strong argument against the push to make sure that no school had more than 50% Black and Puerto Rican kids. [[04:30:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16223.9s)]

*  The State Education Commissioner announced that, [[04:30:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16251.9s)]

*  Diane Ravitch pointed out, [[04:31:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16279.9s)]
*  Diane Ravitch pointed out, [[04:31:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16284.9s)]

*  And so instead they shifted their focus to where it probably should have been all along, away from helping to get the motivated minority of ghetto kids out of the neighborhood into white schools and instead trying to actually improve conditions in ghetto schools, as well as building new schools to alleviate overcrowding. [[04:32:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16338.9s)]
*  One of the schools slated to be built was called Intermediate School 201 or IS 201 in East Harlem. [[04:32:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16361.9s)]
*  And IS 201 was a political lightning rod from the very beginning. [[04:32:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16373.9s)]
*  Black activists in the city actually tried to block it being built because building new schools in the ghetto, they thought, was a cop out from pursuing integration. [[04:33:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16380.9s)]
*  Even though at $5 million, the school was set to be the most expensive school in New York City, the brutalist design of the place made it look like a prison. [[04:33:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16390.9s)]
*  The architectural historian Robert A.M. Stern said it was part of a movement to turn public schools into fortified strongholds, refuges against the decaying city. [[04:33:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16405.9s)]
*  Connato writes, [[04:33:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16420.9s)]
*  The city went to heighten students' concentration by isolating them from their undesirable surroundings, but the design became a symbol for the status of inner-city blacks as invisible members of society. [[04:34:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16450.9s)]
*  Another problem arose when the city chose to name IS 201 the Arthur A. Schomburg School. [[04:34:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16464.9s)]
*  A meeting had been held with the local neighborhood school board to get approval for the name, and they gave their approval. [[04:34:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16472.9s)]
*  But then activist board members who were not at that meeting raised a stink about a school for black and Puerto Rican kids being named after a Jew. [[04:34:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16479.9s)]
*  Which is funny because Arturo Schomburg, as Mr. Schomburg was born, was not Jewish at all. [[04:34:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16489.9s)]
*  He was a well-known, though apparently not well enough known, to the Harlem Parents and Activist Organizations, a well-known historian of black culture who had been born in Puerto Rico to a black mother and a white father. [[04:34:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16496.9s)]
*  Schomburg had moved to New York in 1891. He was part of the Harlem Renaissance. [[04:35:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16510.9s)]
*  He ended up selling his large collection of books and prints and paintings and photographs and so forth to the New York Public Library in 1926. [[04:35:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16516.9s)]
*  And that became the nucleus of the Schomburg Center for Research in Black Culture, which was in Harlem. [[04:35:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16526.9s)]
*  So he was the perfect person to name a mostly black in Puerto Rican Harlem school after. [[04:35:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16533.9s)]
*  But the fact that it took a lot of back and forth with angry parents to explain that gives you an idea of the mood in the city at the time. [[04:35:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16539.9s)]
*  And so while this IS-201 controversy is brewing, the Bundy panel, the Ford Foundation's Bundy panel, is wrapping up its work and preparing a report on the schools for Mayor Lindsay. [[04:35:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16550.9s)]
*  The Bundy panel was made up of wealthy philanthropists, executives from the Ford Foundation, academics who specialized in educational policy, and black in Puerto Rican community activists. [[04:36:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16566.9s)]

[[04:36:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16584.9s)]
*  And McGeorge Bundy had actually requested representatives of those groups to be on the panel, but Mayor Lindsay vetoed it. [[04:36:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16601.9s)]
*  You know, it's just it's how Lindsay viewed the role of government and his role as mayor specifically. [[04:36:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16610.9s)]
*  As far as he was concerned, he did not work for everyone in the city. [[04:36:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16618.9s)]
*  The working and middle class white people did not need him working on their behalf. [[04:37:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16623.9s)]
*  They were fine. [[04:37:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16628.9s)]
*  They had representation through their labor unions, their economic power, their Italian American and their black and white families. [[04:37:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16630.9s)]
*  Their Italian American associations and Irish American and Jewish American associations. [[04:37:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16639.9s)]
*  Those people had all the representation they needed. [[04:37:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16644.9s)]
*  And Lindsay's job as mayor, as he saw it, was to represent the people who had no representation. [[04:37:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16647.9s)]
*  Some very poor whites and all minorities. [[04:37:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16654.9s)]
*  He saw all of those white institutions as he saw them. [[04:37:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16659.9s)]
*  You know, the unions, the churches, the Catholic churches anyway, the community organizations and parents groups. [[04:37:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16664.9s)]
*  He saw them all as obstructionist, self-interested and essentially racist in their foundation. [[04:37:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16670.9s)]
*  And he did not want those people or their representatives on the panel. [[04:37:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16677.9s)]
*  Those people were the problem that the panel was tasked with solving. [[04:38:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16683.9s)]
*  That's just how Lindsay saw things. [[04:38:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16688.9s)]
*  So the panel released its findings in November of 1967. [[04:38:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16692.9s)]
*  And the solutions it proposed were quite radical and involved bringing over a century of school reforms full circle. [[04:38:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16697.9s)]
*  Back when the New York City public school system was created in the 1840s to deal with the hordes of Irish kids suddenly running the streets of New York, [[04:38:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16708.9s)]
*  the Protestant run system had a hard time getting Catholics to put their kids in the schools. [[04:38:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16720.9s)]
*  And so after a fierce battle in both the city and in Albany, which led to more than one Catholic riot, [[04:38:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16726.9s)]
*  the Catholics finally pushed through a reform to radically decentralize the school system. [[04:38:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16736.9s)]
*  Each neighborhood would now have its own local school board that controlled pretty much everything, hiring and firing teachers, [[04:39:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16744.9s)]
*  promotion, salaries, maintenance and building budgets, curriculum, everything. [[04:39:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16752.9s)]
*  The city board of education would have almost no meaningful role at all in how the schools were run. [[04:39:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16758.9s)]
*  Well, the reforms placated the Irish Catholics, but very quickly the schools were taken up into the city's corrupt patronage political system. [[04:39:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16766.9s)]
*  Everything from teachers jobs to building and supply contracts were handed out to politically connected people who happened to have bet on the right horse in the previous election. [[04:39:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16777.9s)]
*  Yet people sitting on some of the school boards in Irish neighborhoods who couldn't even read. [[04:39:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16788.9s)]
*  Half the teachers could do nothing more than read out of a textbook and just have the kids recited back. [[04:39:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16794.9s)]
*  That was that was their capacity as an educator. [[04:40:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16800.9s)]
*  School facilities were starting to fall apart because of corruption and how maintenance contracts and janitorial jobs were handled. [[04:40:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16804.9s)]
*  And so for years, reformers tried and tried to overhaul this system. [[04:40:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16813.9s)]
*  But the genius of the patronage system is that it puts so many people on the payroll. [[04:40:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16819.9s)]
*  It makes sure that so many people have a stake in keeping things the way they are that the reformers can never get past first base. [[04:40:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16825.9s)]
*  Now, the system muddled along mainly because, you know, in the 19th century, [[04:40:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16835.9s)]
*  most Irish kids were dropping out after seventh or eighth grade to go to work to help support the family, [[04:40:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16842.9s)]
*  which was fine for most kids since you could get a decent enough job to get by and have a decent life as long as you knew how to read and write and just do basic arithmetic. [[04:40:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16847.9s)]
*  But then the Jewish and Italian migrations kicked into gear in the 1880s. [[04:40:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16858.9s)]
*  The Italians treated education more or less like the Irish, but not the Jews. [[04:41:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16864.9s)]
*  The Jews were obsessed with education. [[04:41:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16871.9s)]
*  They were not pressuring their kids to drop out after eighth grade to get to work. [[04:41:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16875.9s)]
*  Kids and families who did that were shamed in the Jewish community. [[04:41:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16880.9s)]
*  And Jews wanted as much education as they could possibly get. [[04:41:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16885.9s)]
*  They took advantage of City College. [[04:41:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16890.9s)]
*  New York has a free City College for the city's residents. [[04:41:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16892.9s)]
*  And it got to the point by 1920 that the student population at City College was 85 percent Jewish. [[04:41:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16895.9s)]
*  It was still 60, 65 percent in 1960. [[04:41:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16902.9s)]
*  Their attitude toward education, though, set them up for serious disappointment when they first got here and got a look at the condition of the school system. [[04:41:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16907.9s)]
*  The millions of new Jewish and Italian students completely overwhelmed the system. [[04:41:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16918.9s)]
*  And the corrupt, sclerotic local school boards were completely incapable of dealing with the crisis. [[04:42:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16924.9s)]
*  The physical condition of the schools got to be really bad. [[04:42:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16932.9s)]
*  Teachers were unable to manage overcrowded classes. [[04:42:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16936.9s)]
*  Everybody knew something had to change. [[04:42:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16941.9s)]
*  But the current system stakeholders still fought reform. [[04:42:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16944.9s)]
*  You know, incompetent teachers in the system, they had secure jobs in the patronage system. [[04:42:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16948.9s)]
*  And they knew they were going to be in trouble if suddenly they had to compete in a merit based system. [[04:42:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16955.9s)]
*  The members of the local school boards had a lot of influence in their communities because of their ability to hand out jobs and contracts. [[04:42:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16961.9s)]
*  And none of these people wanted to give that up. [[04:42:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16970.9s)]
*  But this time, the reformers, who had always been mostly WASPs, this time the reformers had one of the immigrant groups on their side. [[04:42:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16973.9s)]
*  New York Jews were Democrats, just like all other immigrants. [[04:43:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16981.9s)]
*  But their concern for education lined them up on the side of the Republicans and the reform Democrats on that particular issue. [[04:43:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16985.9s)]
*  And so in 1896, they were finally able to completely overhaul the public school system. [[04:43:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16993.9s)]
*  They eliminated the local boards altogether and centralized all authority in a single city board of education. [[04:43:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=16999.9s)]
*  Teachers and administrators were no longer hired, fired, placed or promoted based on who they knew. [[04:43:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17008.9s)]
*  They all had to take a pretty serious civil service exam. [[04:43:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17017.9s)]
*  And the ones who scored the best got their pick of assignments and promotions. [[04:43:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17021.9s)]
*  People who sat on the board of education and the bureaucrats who staffed it, they were trained, credentialed education professionals, [[04:43:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17026.9s)]
*  not people who got their job because they knew a guy. [[04:43:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17036.9s)]
*  It was a strict meritocratic system. [[04:43:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17039.9s)]
*  Well, this opened up teaching as a career opportunity for New York Jews who were confident that they could outcompete other working and middle class groups [[04:44:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17043.9s)]
*  for those jobs as long as the system was based on merit. [[04:44:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17053.9s)]
*  And they were right. They did outcompete everyone else. [[04:44:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17058.9s)]
*  By 1920, more than half the teachers and administrators in New York public schools were Jewish. [[04:44:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17062.9s)]
*  Over the next few decades, that would grow until about 70 to 75 percent of all teachers and administrators were Jews in New York City. [[04:44:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17070.9s)]
*  The New York City public school system was by the 1950s. [[04:44:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17081.9s)]
*  It's not really an exaggeration to say it was a Jewish operation. [[04:44:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17085.9s)]
*  But here's the thing. [[04:44:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17090.9s)]
*  Nobody complained because the Jews did a great job. [[04:44:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17092.9s)]
*  The period from World War One up to about 1955, 1960 is remembered by everyone as the Golden Age of the New York City public school system. [[04:44:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17096.9s)]
*  It was the best in the country, far and away. [[04:45:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17107.9s)]
*  And it was the model that other cities looked to when they wanted to improve their own schools. [[04:45:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17109.9s)]
*  Nobody was particularly concerned about Jews having so much control over this municipal function because, again, that's how the city had always worked. [[04:45:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17115.9s)]
*  The police and fire departments were mostly Irish. [[04:45:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17124.9s)]
*  The Transit Workers Union was mostly Irish. [[04:45:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17127.9s)]
*  Always run by the Irish, the police department anyway. [[04:45:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17131.9s)]
*  Still today, even today, something like nine out of the last ten NYPD police chiefs have been Irish. [[04:45:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17134.9s)]
*  Italians controlled sanitation and construction contracts, and the Jews controlled the schools. [[04:45:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17142.9s)]
*  Everybody had a piece of the pie, and nobody really complained too much about it as long as everybody did their jobs. [[04:45:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17150.9s)]
*  Like I said, that Golden Age came to an end by 1960 when another huge wave of migrants, blacks from the South and Puerto Ricans, flooded into the system and overwhelmed it once again. [[04:45:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17157.9s)]
*  So what the Ford Foundation recommended was that the city undo those 1896 reforms and radically reduce the power of the city board of education and devolve control of the schools back down to local boards. [[04:46:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17171.9s)]
*  Now there were white parent groups, parent groups from white areas, who had been fighting for community control of schools for years. [[04:46:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17186.9s)]
*  And if they had been invited to participate in the process, it probably would have helped smooth out the transition to a decentralized system, but they were not invited. [[04:46:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17196.9s)]
*  The Teachers Union, they had been also advocating for a certain amount of decentralization. [[04:46:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17206.9s)]
*  Many people felt that the system had just grown too big for a single board of education to effectively manage. [[04:46:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17214.9s)]
*  And that if local boards were stood up to represent parents and students, the teachers would be able to respond more precisely to the needs of different communities. [[04:47:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17221.9s)]
*  But the teachers wanted nothing to do with what the Bundy panel was talking about, which they said was not decentralization, but balkanization. [[04:47:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17231.9s)]
*  The proposal is anti-professional. It would encourage local vigilantes to harass teachers. [[04:47:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17251.9s)]
*  No teacher with professional integrity could teach in such a district. [[04:47:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17257.9s)]
*  The union charged that so-called community control, at least as formulated by the Bundy panel, would not actually empower parents, but local militants and activists, because those people were already organized and would make sure that their people got control of the school boards. [[04:47:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17263.9s)]
*  The union charged that community control was just a euphemism for a return to the old ethnic spoil system, or in this case, a racial spoil system. [[04:48:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17283.9s)]
*  For years, black militants had been making the case that black students should only be taught by black teachers in schools run by black administrators. [[04:48:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17295.9s)]
*  And the union warned that bringing race into hiring, firing, promoting, and placing teachers would lead to conflict, and that it would erode standards and open the door to manipulation and corruption. [[04:48:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17304.9s)]
*  But according to the African American Teachers Association, the ATA, an ethnic spoil system was already in place, one which benefited the white, mostly Jewish, educators who had long since left the neighborhoods they were supposed to be serving. [[04:48:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17318.9s)]
*  Most of all, the union was concerned that devolving so much power to the boards of laymen would have the effect of invalidating their contractual rights that the union had negotiated for the teachers with the city. [[04:48:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17336.9s)]
*  So a self-appointed People's Board of Education was stood up by a group of black and white militants, and they released a statement that read, [[04:49:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17348.9s)]
*  The People's Board plan proposes that all appropriations will come directly to the local school board. School personnel are to be hired by community supervisory bodies, and program and policy for education to be worked out by each community, using the school system's central headquarters merely as a resource center. [[04:49:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17360.9s)]
*  In other words, what they wanted was not different districts. They wanted effectively separate school systems in each district. [[04:49:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17380.9s)]
*  The People's Board at one point took over the Board of Education's meeting room by creating a ruckus and forcing the real board out of the room. And the minister who led the People's Board made their goals very clear. He said, We're trying to get rid of the Board of Education. There is no other solution. [[04:49:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17389.9s)]
*  Vincent Canado writes, [[04:50:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17408.9s)]
*  Even more troubling was the growing intimidation of white principals and teachers in inner city schools. In 1966, there were 213 attacks on public school teachers. The following year, there were 224. [[04:50:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17411.9s)]
*  In December 1966, a group of 30 protesters blockaded the office of Kate Tuchman, a white Jewish principal of Public School 125 on the border of Morningside Heights in Harlem. [[04:50:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17426.9s)]
*  Earlier, a group of militants had asked Tuchman to waive her right to be principal. They barricaded her in her office for nearly an hour, waiting for her answer to their request. [[04:50:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17438.9s)]
*  Two of the people involved, Babette Edwards and Robert Nickell, were both activists in the IS-201 controversy and the People's Board of Education. [[04:50:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17449.9s)]
*  Their appearance at PS125 suggested that the protests came not from parents at the grassroots, but from a highly motivated and vocal band of militants. [[04:50:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17459.9s)]
*  The following spring, black militants in Brooklyn engaged in low-level terrorism against white principals and teachers in schools in Brownsville and Bedford-Stuyvesant. [[04:51:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17470.9s)]
*  At PS284, 50 predominantly Jewish teachers refused to work after a flier attacking teachers was distributed. [[04:51:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17480.9s)]
*  Written on some of the notes were messages such as, [[04:51:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17489.9s)]
*  Out of here, you no-good Jew bastard! And, [[04:51:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17492.9s)]
*  Don't come back here in September if you know what's good for you. [[04:51:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17496.9s)]
*  Two days later, the principal of PS284, William Emmer, asked to be transferred out of the school. [[04:51:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17500.9s)]
*  He and nine other teachers had been singled out by Brooklyn Core, the Congress on Racial Equality, led by Sonny Carson and the Brownsville Community Council. [[04:51:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17507.9s)]
*  By June, 30 of the 50 teachers at PS284 asked to be transferred out of the school. [[04:51:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17516.9s)]
*  The previous week, Harry Levine, principal of Junior High School 258 in Bedford-Stuyvesant, requested a transfer after Brooklyn Core demanded he leave the school. [[04:52:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17523.9s)]
*  Levine said he had been threatened. Core asked all principals in Brooklyn's ghetto schools to create a plan to improve reading scores and hire more black teachers. [[04:52:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17533.9s)]
*  The principals obliged, but the response was unsatisfactory to Core, and Carson said his group considered all but five of the 32 principals in the area to be fired. [[04:52:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17543.9s)]
*  Michael Romano, president of the Elementary School Principals Association, wrote that black radicals really don't want white principals in the schools. [[04:52:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17554.9s)]
*  Carson said, if the superintendent thinks we're kidding, he had better wait until September and see what happens when those teachers, those principals, try to come back to our community. [[04:52:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17564.9s)]
*  One of the worst examples of the intimidation of school personnel occurred on January 19, 1968. [[04:52:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17574.9s)]
*  Four black men entered Junior High School 117 in the Clinton Hill section of Brooklyn, asking to see the principal, John O'Connor. [[04:53:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17582.9s)]
*  When O'Connor arrived, the men, none of whom had children at the school, called him a honky and pushed him. [[04:53:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17590.9s)]
*  When the acting assistant principal, George Elias, stepped in, he was pushed. [[04:53:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17597.9s)]
*  Robert Goldberg, head of the Social Studies Department, became involved. [[04:53:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17602.9s)]
*  One secretary who witnessed the fight called it a wild Western brawl, with fists flying everywhere. [[04:53:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17606.9s)]
*  O'Connor, 47, and Goldberg, 29, were knocked out, while Elias, 45, was knocked down. [[04:53:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17612.9s)]
*  The secretary fainted. [[04:53:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17619.9s)]
*  Some parent and community representatives seemed to condone the violence. [[04:53:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17621.9s)]
*  Margaret Campbell, chairman of the Parents Organization of District 13 in Bedford-Stuyvesant, said, [[04:53:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17626.9s)]
*  We don't say that anybody should beat up anybody, but we also say that nobody should have to feel they have to beat someone. [[04:53:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17632.9s)]
*  This system has made people feel like this. [[04:53:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17639.9s)]
*  While we don't condone it, we're in a position where we cannot condemn it, knowing their root causes. [[04:54:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=17642.9s)]

*  McCoy wrote an article for an education journal that spring that read in part, [[05:09:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18599.9s)]
*  One of McCoy's first acts as head of the Ocean Hill Brownsville district was to appoint Herman Ferguson, [[05:10:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18630.9s)]
*  the man indicted for plotting to kill the two moderate civil rights activists who were still out on bail, as principal of one of the schools. [[05:10:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18639.9s)]
*  Ferguson had a long and public record of extremist racial rhetoric, even beyond that IS-201 Malcolm rally. [[05:10:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18648.9s)]
*  In 1967, he wrote in the newsletter for the African American Teachers Association, [[05:10:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18658.9s)]
*  Black teachers must begin to assume our natural role as a revolutionary force in the just struggle for liberation [[05:11:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18664.9s)]
*  that is now going on in the third world that encompasses black America as well as Latin America, Asia, and Africa. [[05:11:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18672.9s)]
*  In March 1968, Ferguson published an article in The Guardian in which he wrote that it wasn't enough for black people to get control of their schools. [[05:11:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18681.9s)]
*  Once we really take this control, he said, we must be prepared to teach our black youth how to survive in the hostile society that we do not yet control. [[05:11:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18691.9s)]
*  In the article, Ferguson described his ideal school. He said, students would learn in classrooms, [[05:11:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18701.9s)]
*  adorned with pictures of great black fighters like Malcolm X, Marcus Garvey, and Muhammad Ali. [[05:11:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18709.9s)]
*  They would start the day pledging allegiance to the black, red, and green Pan-African flag and reciting a poem by LaRoy Jones. [[05:11:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18716.9s)]
*  Morning classes would consist of physical exercise, martial arts training, instruction in gun weaponry, gun handling, and gun safety. [[05:12:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18724.9s)]
*  Loudspeakers, he said, placed in the ceilings, would continuously bathe the black student with the quiet sound of Malcolm X preaching, [[05:12:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18737.9s)]
*  LaRoy Jones reading one of his poems, Aretha Franklin singing a soul song, and other black heroes speaking to him and filling him with a constant pride in his blackness. [[05:12:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18747.9s)]
*  He said math classes would take a practical approach and would teach students things like wind velocity and muzzle velocity and other mathematical considerations involved in firing, repairing, and making weapons. [[05:12:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18759.9s)]
*  Home economics would teach students first aid and how to survive off the surrounding environment when all food and fuel supply lines into the black community are cut off. [[05:12:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18775.9s)]
*  Shop class would instruct students in things like making electronic timers and gunsmithing. [[05:13:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18788.9s)]
*  As Canado says, all this could be dismissed as the quasi-fascistic dreaming of a crank, except that it was written by a man deemed by Rody McCoy of becoming a principal. [[05:13:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18795.9s)]
*  And Fred Siegel wrote, [[05:13:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18807.9s)]
*  The ATA notes historian Jerry Podair saw universalism as a Jewish liberal trick, a means by which Jews who did better academically by white standards would continue to hold on to jobs in the Board of Education. [[05:13:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18837.9s)]
*  They pitted that which is private and ethnic as against that which is public and culture blind. [[05:14:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18858.9s)]
*  They insisted that racial cultures were so separate that only black teachers could teach black children effectively. [[05:14:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18865.9s)]
*  Individualism and personal merit, the ATA argued, was a myth perpetuated by whites to create, quote, black versions of the white middle class or black Anglo-Saxons. [[05:14:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18873.9s)]
*  The ATA called for an alternative black value system based on principles of collective work and responsibility, cooperative economics and unity. [[05:14:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18887.9s)]
*  They said giftedness in black children could be measured by a willingness to challenge authority, end quote. [[05:14:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18898.9s)]
*  In April 1968, of course, Martin Luther King Jr. was assassinated in Memphis. [[05:15:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18908.9s)]
*  And black students rioted in schools across New York City. [[05:15:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18917.9s)]
*  A female student in the Ocean Hill Brownsville district named Karima Jordan said, We just threw chairs around, wrote on the walls, avenge King, kill whitey. [[05:15:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18922.9s)]
*  Students rampaged through the halls and many teachers had to lock themselves inside their classrooms to keep safe. [[05:15:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18934.9s)]
*  A black nationalist teacher named Leslie Campbell, one of the leaders in the ATA, who had been brought into one of the schools in the Ocean Hill Brownsville district by Rody McCoy, [[05:15:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18943.9s)]
*  was asked to speak to students at a school assembly to try to calm things down. [[05:15:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18956.9s)]
*  Instead, he told the students, Brothers and sisters, you have to stop fighting among yourselves. [[05:16:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18960.9s)]
*  You have your money and finally get enough for a leather jacket and your brother steals it. [[05:16:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18966.9s)]
*  You've got to get your minds together. If you steal, steal from those who have it. [[05:16:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18971.9s)]
*  Stop fighting among yourselves. When the enemy taps you on the shoulder, send them to the cemetery and you know who your enemy is, end quote. [[05:16:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18976.9s)]
*  The speech fired up the students so much that they tore through the halls, attacking any white students and teachers that they could corner. [[05:16:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18985.9s)]
*  One white female teacher was punched and her hair was torn out and her clothes were ripped off. [[05:16:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=18993.9s)]
*  Well, despite everything, the UFT was trying at first to be accommodative. [[05:16:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19001.9s)]
*  A few teachers were uncomfortable with the direction of the program at JHS 271 in the Ocean Hill Brownsville district. [[05:16:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19009.9s)]
*  And so McCoy demanded that they be transferred to another school and they agreed and the union agreed to expedite the move. [[05:16:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19016.9s)]
*  Then the new Community Control Board began implementing curriculum changes, which included advocacy for black separatism and revolution. [[05:17:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19025.9s)]
*  Pictures of Malcolm X, Elijah Muhammad and black nationalist slogans went up on the walls of classrooms taught by black radical teachers. [[05:17:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19035.9s)]
*  A few black teachers began holding extracurricular training in martial arts and guerrilla warfare tactics and effectively turned their classrooms into training centers for black militants. [[05:17:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19046.9s)]
*  White kids were being openly discriminated against by many black teachers. [[05:17:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19058.9s)]
*  Classes sometimes became struggle sessions with white students being used as foils for the teachers' racial harangues. [[05:17:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19064.9s)]
*  More white teachers started becoming alarmed at what was happening. [[05:17:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19073.9s)]
*  And this time McCoy didn't wait for cooperation from the teachers union to act. [[05:17:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19078.9s)]
*  He summarily fired 19 UFT teachers and administrators for ideological noncompliance. [[05:18:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19082.9s)]
*  Asked why the situation hadn't been handled with more tact, one radical said that confrontation with the Board of Education and the teachers union had to come sooner or later. [[05:18:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19089.9s)]
*  And so it was better to start the fight in the spring to hang the threat of summer riots over the heads of city officials. [[05:18:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19100.9s)]
*  They learned from experience that the city was so desperate to avoid a riot that in the end they would always buckle. [[05:18:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19107.9s)]
*  And if they could get away with firing these teachers, then they would set a precedent that would carry forward into the future. [[05:18:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19116.9s)]
*  McCoy didn't even pretend that the firings had anything to do with performance. [[05:18:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19124.9s)]
*  He admitted openly that they had been fired for what he called their politics. [[05:18:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19129.9s)]
*  All the fired teachers were white except for one black teacher who was a victim of mistaken identity. [[05:18:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19133.9s)]
*  And that teacher was reinstated as soon as the mistake was recognized. [[05:19:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19140.9s)]
*  Such a flagrant violation of the teachers' contract with the city forced the union to do something. [[05:19:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19145.9s)]
*  Al Shanker, the leader of the union, said that if they didn't take a stand now, then there was no point in even having a teachers union. [[05:19:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19153.9s)]
*  And so after giving the city fair warning and a chance to reinstate the teachers, [[05:19:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19161.9s)]
*  UFT teachers across the city walked off the job in protest, promising to shut down the schools until the fired teachers were back in their classrooms. [[05:19:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19166.9s)]
*  You know, in city after city and neighborhood after neighborhood, racial militants and their elite liberal backers had just swept aside the opposition of the white ethnics trying to resist the changes in their communities, just swept them aside. [[05:19:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19177.9s)]
*  But their long run of success in the 1960s had made them overconfident. [[05:19:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19196.9s)]
*  They were so used to everybody buckling and giving in and surrendering to all their demands when it came down to do what we want or there will be violence. [[05:20:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19202.9s)]
*  They were so used to the city's buckling that they became overconfident. [[05:20:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19213.9s)]
*  And by picking a fight with the teachers union, they had bitten off more than they could chew. [[05:20:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19218.9s)]
*  This time, it was the activists who would be put on the back foot, and they found themselves unable to control the terms of the debate over decentralization, even with the Lindsay administration and most of the prestige press on their side. [[05:20:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19224.9s)]
*  See McCoy's strategy of getting militants to focus on the teachers Jewishness was a huge tactical mistake. [[05:20:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19240.9s)]
*  By choosing that path, he transformed a conflict that in other circumstances would have been framed as blacks versus whites into a fight between blacks and Jews. [[05:20:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19250.9s)]
*  And by doing that, he ran right into the teeth of the teachers strongest defenses. [[05:21:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19261.9s)]
*  In the current climate in 1968, the teachers whiteness was their vulnerability. [[05:21:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19269.9s)]
*  But their Jewishness was a strength. [[05:21:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19276.9s)]
*  If the battle had been understood as black versus white, then the radicals probably would have routed the white teachers. [[05:21:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19280.9s)]
*  But by focusing on the teachers Jewishness, that mobilized the Jewish community against them. [[05:21:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19287.9s)]
*  In the former case, the teachers would have been on the defensive fighting off accusations of white racism. [[05:21:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19294.9s)]
*  But as it happened, they were able to go on the offensive, returning fire with well substantiated accusations of anti-Semitism. [[05:21:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19299.9s)]
*  The mostly Jewish teachers union against 70, 75 percent of all the teachers and administrators in the public school system were Jewish. [[05:21:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19309.9s)]
*  The same was true in the union and in the union leadership. [[05:21:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19318.9s)]
*  These people had taken in left-wing politics and organizing with their mother's milk. [[05:22:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19322.9s)]
*  Their politics typically ranged from anti-Soviet Trotskyites to New Deal Democrats, and they had always supported civil rights and racial integration. [[05:22:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19330.9s)]
*  Al Shanker, the union leader, and many other union executives and members had made the trip down to Alabama in 1965 to go join Martin Luther King's march to Selma. [[05:22:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19341.9s)]
*  They knew all the militants tricks better than the militants themselves did. [[05:22:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19353.9s)]
*  And they were not people to be easily cowed with frivolous accusations of racism, especially when their accusers were using language reminiscent of old world anti-Semitism. [[05:22:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19358.9s)]
*  Probably no other group in the country was as well organized as New York Jews. [[05:22:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19370.9s)]
*  They had built a network of charities and jobs programs and youth summer camps, religious institutions, educational institutions, anti-defamation organizations, and they could all work together with military precision when they really needed to. [[05:22:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19378.9s)]
*  And so this was the first time that black militants ran into a group of card carrying liberals who were actually willing and able to stand their ground. [[05:23:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19396.9s)]
*  The school year ended without the question of the fired teachers being resolved. [[05:23:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19409.9s)]
*  We're talking June 1968. So the 67-68 school year ended. [[05:23:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19416.9s)]
*  And during the summer, the union went to court and a judge ruled that the firing of the teachers was completely illegal, violated the teachers contract with the city, and to reinstate them. [[05:23:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19424.9s)]
*  But McCoy said he was going to ignore the judge and he would use whatever means were necessary to keep those teachers away from his school. [[05:23:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19435.9s)]
*  Some 150 cities across the country burned in the summer of 68. [[05:24:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19443.9s)]
*  New York managed to avoid the worst of it, but everyone's attention was still focused on the battle over the schools. [[05:24:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19449.9s)]
*  And as the new school year approached in the fall, everybody expected a confrontation. [[05:24:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19456.9s)]
*  McCoy was still promising to keep the teachers out of the school. [[05:24:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19463.9s)]

*  The union immediately countered that the strike would indeed go forward if the teachers were not brought back. [[05:24:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19488.9s)]
*  And so that night, the Board of Education announced that the teachers would be reinstated. [[05:24:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19493.9s)]
*  But Rody McCoy said, if they return to campus, I can't guarantee their safety, which he meant as a threat. [[05:24:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19498.9s)]
*  But even if he hadn't, it was probably true. He could not guarantee their safety. [[05:25:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19504.9s)]

*  The mayor's office, the Ocean Hill Brownsville governing board, the Board of Education, the Commissioner of Education, the superintendent and the New York Times and most of the major media all supported decentralization and community control. *  He poked it at us and went ratatatat back to Connato. [[05:28:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19706.9s)]
*  Teachers believe McCoy had orchestrated the whole scene. [[05:28:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19711.9s)]

*  Now, Mayor John Lindsay did not get along with any union leaders. [[05:29:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19782.9s)]
*  Actually, that's a huge understatement. He could not stand them and they could not stand him. [[05:29:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19788.9s)]
*  He saw them as narrow minded, bigoted power brokers, protecting privileges that they had accrued through years of complicit city government. [[05:29:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19794.9s)]
*  And they saw him as an insufferable, self-righteous, limousine liberal. [[05:30:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19805.9s)]
*  That term actually came into being to describe John Lindsay, who was bigoted against working class whites and knew nothing about what happened in his own city outside of his posh Manhattan neighborhood. [[05:30:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19810.9s)]
*  In his first year in office, Lindsay had picked a fight with the mostly Irish Transit Workers Union in the city. [[05:30:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19822.9s)]
*  And that led to a strike that shut down the subway system for 13 days and cost the city hundreds of millions in lost economic activity. [[05:30:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19830.9s)]
*  The next year, he picked a fight with the mostly Italian Sanitation Workers Union. [[05:30:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19838.9s)]
*  And that led to a strike that ended with 100,000 tons of uncollected garbage piled up on the streets of New York. [[05:30:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19843.9s)]
*  Both of those strikes became bitter and personal between Lindsay and the union leaders, and both times the governor of New York state, Nelson Rockefeller, had to step in and impose a settlement. [[05:30:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19851.9s)]
*  When the garbage men went on strike, Lindsay actually requested that the governor send in the National Guard to come pick up trash, but only to pick it up in black and Puerto Rican neighborhoods. [[05:31:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19863.9s)]
*  Because as far as Lindsay was concerned, the working and middle class whites in Queens and South Brooklyn and Staten Island, those people all supported the sanitation workers strike. [[05:31:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19874.9s)]
*  And so they were complicit in what was happening. Rockefeller refused to do that. [[05:31:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19884.9s)]
*  Lindsay also failed to avoid work stoppages by hospital workers, welfare department social workers, and the state's health department. [[05:31:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19892.9s)]
*  And he failed to stop job actions by the police and fire departments. [[05:31:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19901.9s)]

*  And journalist Jack Newfield, who started out as one of the mayor's most adoring admirers, but later became more critical, said, [[05:32:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19969.9s)]
*  And so by the time the confrontation with the teachers union came about, Lindsay's reputation with the city's unions was already set in stone. [[05:33:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=19991.9s)]
*  But he hated UFT president Al Shanker more than anybody else. [[05:33:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20000.9s)]
*  In an article on the 50th anniversary of the Battle of Ocean Hill, Brownsville, Vincent Cannato and journalist Jerry Podare, or historian Jerry Podare rather, wrote, quote, [[05:33:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20006.9s)]
*  Lindsay's view of the outside Manhattan was perfunctory and who, in the words of a contemporary observer, doesn't understand the life of a mailman or a cop, [[05:33:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20021.9s)]
*  Appeared to view municipal politics as a zero-sum game in which the gains of the city's middle class had come at the expense of the minority poor. [[05:33:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20030.9s)]
*  To Lindsay, New York's public sector unions and the white ethnic groups that predominated in them were self-interested impediments to racial justice in the city. [[05:34:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20040.9s)]
*  In contemporary lingo, Lindsay saw these working class whites as deeply laden with white privilege. [[05:34:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20049.9s)]
*  Albert Shanker, the grim-vissaged UFT president, was the labor leader Lindsay liked least, a sentiment fully reciprocated by the Queen's bred son of Russian Jewish immigrants. [[05:34:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20056.9s)]
*  Lindsay viewed the brusque Shanker as déclassé, vulgar, and worse. [[05:34:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20068.9s)]
*  He was the only person whom Mary Lindsay, the city's first lady, banned from the private living quarters at Gracie Mansion, the mayor's official residence. [[05:34:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20073.9s)]
*  At one point during negotiations at City Hall, Shanker deeply offended Lindsay's sense of decorum by putting his feet on the mayor's desk and revealing his sagging socks. [[05:34:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20082.9s)]
*  To the Lindsay people, Shanker and his union failed their test of selflessness and concern for the public interest. [[05:34:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20092.9s)]
*  They were simply power brokers, looking to put their own power ahead of the public good. [[05:34:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20099.9s)]

*  And so for the third time, the UFT went back on strike on October 14th and they would not come back until well into November. [[05:39:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20395.9s)]
*  The union published a full page ad in the Times that asked, [[05:40:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20405.9s)]
