*  Finally, just as it had in the previous two strikes of the transit and sanitation workers, the state of New York got involved. [[05:43:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20590.9s)]
*  After a 27-hour marathon negotiation, a settlement was reached between Mayor Lindsay and Al Shanker with the state commissioner of education acting as guarantor of the agreement. [[05:43:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20599.9s)]
*  It was not an agreement Lindsay was happy with, but the state told them that he was going to make an agreement or the state was going to make one for him. [[05:43:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20612.9s)]
*  According to the agreement, the Ocean Hill Brownsville principals and teachers who were hired in violation of established regulations were all to be removed. [[05:43:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20621.9s)]
*  A state trustee would be appointed to oversee the district, taking it out of the hands not only of the governing board, but out of the hands of New York City altogether. [[05:43:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20631.9s)]
*  A three-person panel was to be set up to monitor the treatment of teachers throughout the system, and Rhodey McCoy would be allowed to remain as a disempowered administrator of the Ocean Hill Brownsville district if he agreed to abide by the settlement, which they knew he would not. [[05:44:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20642.9s)]
*  And so the agreement was effectively to remove Rhodey McCoy as well. [[05:44:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20659.9s)]
*  And the governing board overseeing the district was to be abolished, and the community control experiment came to an end. [[05:44:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20665.9s)]
*  Some of the teachers felt that after everything that they had been through, the settlement didn't go nearly far enough, but the overwhelming majority signed off on it. [[05:44:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20674.9s)]
*  On the other side, militant leaders complained that the mayor had laid down in total capitulation to the union, but he really had no choice. [[05:44:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20683.9s)]
*  On Tuesday, November 19, New York City teachers returned to their schools for the first time in five weeks. [[05:44:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20692.9s)]
*  The administrative victory was not the end of the matter, however. [[05:45:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20701.9s)]
*  ATA leader Leslie Campbell and Brooklyn Corps chairman Sonny Carson, both of whom had been very prominent in the student rebellions and led student riots in different parts of the city, created the citywide student strike committee and began to organize and incite violence and vandalism at schools throughout the city. [[05:45:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20707.9s)]
*  On December 2, they led hundreds of students as they threw rocks and bottles at police who were providing security for the Ocean Hill Brownsville teachers, many of whom had had serious threats made against their lives. [[05:45:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20730.9s)]
*  Several teachers had threats the police took so seriously that they received around the clock protection at their homes. [[05:45:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20744.9s)]
*  Hundreds of black students stormed through schools throughout the city, shutting several of them down and destroying property in and around the schools. [[05:45:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20751.9s)]
*  Student riots occurred in four out of five New York boroughs, and they continued every day for the entire week. [[05:46:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20760.9s)]
*  About 50 adult militants, led by deposed members of the abolished governing board, shoved their way into JHS 271. [[05:46:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20768.9s)]
*  They barged into classrooms, started screaming at union teachers in front of their students. [[05:46:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20777.9s)]
*  The PTA president was part of the group and she stormed into a classroom telling the teacher to get out. [[05:46:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20783.9s)]
*  And when the teacher wouldn't budge, teacher was a female, she was punched in the face. [[05:46:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20788.9s)]
*  Two other teachers were attacked in a similar fashion. [[05:46:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20793.9s)]
*  Well, then on December 26, 1968, Leslie Campbell, the ATA teacher who was at the center of so many of the of the problems over the course of the year, [[05:46:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20798.9s)]
*  was interviewed by Julius Lester on a popular black radio station out of Harlem. [[05:46:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20810.9s)]
*  And he had brought with him several poems written by his black students, and Lester asked him to read one of them. [[05:46:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20817.9s)]
*  The poem he chose was titled Anti-Semitism, a tribute to Albert Schenker. [[05:47:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20824.9s)]
*  Your escape from tyranny. I'm sick of seeing in everything I do about the murder of six million Jews. [[05:47:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20854.9s)]
*  Hitler's reign lasted for only 15 years. For that period of time, you shed crocodile tears. [[05:47:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20861.9s)]
*  My suffering lasted for 400 years, Jew boy, and the white man only let me play with his toys. [[05:47:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20868.9s)]
*  Jew boy, you took my religion and adopted it for you. But you know that black people were the original Hebrews. [[05:47:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20875.9s)]
*  When the UN made Israel a free independent state, little four and five year old boys threw hand grenades. [[05:48:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20883.9s)]
*  They hated the black Arabs with all their might. And you, Jew boy, said it was all right. [[05:48:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20890.9s)]
*  Then you came to America, land of the free, and took over the school system to perpetuate white supremacy. [[05:48:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20896.9s)]
*  Guess you know, Jew boy, there's only one reason you made it. You had a clean white face, colorless and faded. [[05:48:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20903.9s)]
*  I hated you, Jew boy, because your hang up was the Torah. And my only hang up was my color. [[05:48:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20912.9s)]
*  Well, Jewish organizations made sure that that poem was reprinted in full in a full page ad in the New York Times. [[05:48:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20921.9s)]
*  The following year, 1969, saw an explosion of attacks against Jewish houses of worship. [[05:48:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20930.9s)]
*  Kinnado writes, [[05:48:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20937.9s)]
*  There were 90 crimes at houses of worship in the city. In 1969, there were 1,039 such attacks. [[05:49:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20967.9s)]
*  Of those attacks, 633 were burglaries, 50 were arson, and 356 were vandalism and criminal mischief. [[05:49:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20982.9s)]
*  Now there was a dispute at the time, and there kind of still is among people who care about this stuff, [[05:49:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20992.9s)]
*  whether that increase in attacks were, whether it was an organized effort to intimidate the city's Jews, [[05:49:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=20998.9s)]
*  or if they were just part of the overall increase in chaos and violent crime in New York. [[05:50:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21005.9s)]
*  But the Jews in the city, they didn't need to be told what it was about. [[05:50:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21012.9s)]
*  As far as they were concerned, there was no question about it. It was obvious. [[05:50:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21017.9s)]
*  A Jewish writer named Meir Kahane was the editor of the Jewish Press, [[05:50:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21021.9s)]
*  and he started to receive a lot of letters from Jews around the city with stories of being harassed and attacked. [[05:50:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21027.9s)]
*  And so in response, he created the Jewish Defense League, which subsequently became known to the FBI as a violent extremist organization. [[05:50:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21034.9s)]
*  One study of Jewish terrorism in the US between 1980 and 1985 showed that 15 of the 18 Jews indicted for terrorist acts were members of the JDL. [[05:50:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21044.9s)]
*  These were very serious people. They weren't afraid of anybody. [[05:50:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21058.9s)]
*  When black militants showed up to intimidate and harass a Jewish business or public person, [[05:51:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21061.9s)]
*  the JDL would show up and go toe to toe with them in the streets, and if they wanted to fight, they'd have a fight. [[05:51:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21066.9s)]
*  To this day, the JDL is suspected in the 1972 bombing of a Manhattan theater that killed two people and injured several others. [[05:51:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21074.9s)]
*  But meanwhile, violence just escalated in the schools after the settlement was reached between the teachers union and the city. [[05:51:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21085.9s)]
*  It just got worse and worse. [[05:51:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21092.9s)]
*  Majority black schools had long been unsafe for white students, [[05:51:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21094.9s)]
*  but now they were unsafe for white teachers and other adults. [[05:51:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21099.9s)]
*  Harold Salzman, who was a teacher and union leader at the time, described the decline of his school, Franklin K. Lane High School in South Brooklyn. [[05:51:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21103.9s)]
*  Lane was located in an integrated neighborhood with about 50-50 white and POC. [[05:51:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21118.9s)]
*  But then the city, in all its wisdom, decided to use Lane as a dumping ground for ghetto kids in an effort to placate black parents who were demanding integration of their own schools. [[05:52:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21123.9s)]
*  The city had wanted to build more schools in the ghetto area to alleviate overcrowding at the existing schools, but the activists did not want new black schools. [[05:52:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21136.9s)]
*  They wanted integrated schools. [[05:52:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21144.9s)]
*  And so Lane went from having about a 50-50 racial distribution to being mostly black. [[05:52:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21146.9s)]
*  And as the situation deteriorated in the school, white parents pulled their kids out and you had this school that was almost all black in a neighborhood that was about 50-50. [[05:52:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21153.9s)]
*  Now, Lane was built to accommodate just about 3,000 students, but by the late 60s, it would have over 5,000. [[05:52:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21165.9s)]
*  This is just one example of the illogical outcomes of the city's policies. [[05:52:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21173.9s)]
*  As the local white kids were pulled out of school and sent somewhere else to private school or another district, parent participation and involvement in the school completely collapsed, since the kids being bussed in were from far away and the parents weren't making the trip for parents night. [[05:52:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21179.9s)]
*  As the demographics of the school changed, so did academic standards. [[05:53:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21197.9s)]
*  Physics and chemistry were dropped from the curriculum, as were foreign languages except for Spanish. [[05:53:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21202.9s)]
*  Honors classes were eliminated altogether. [[05:53:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21209.9s)]
*  As the atmosphere in the school became more hostile, students stopped participating in sports and extracurricular activities, many of which were eliminated. [[05:53:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21213.9s)]
*  Lane had a champion basketball team, but they couldn't get anyone to come to the games. [[05:53:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21221.9s)]
*  Hard drugs had also changed life in ghetto schools. [[05:53:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21227.9s)]
*  The official in charge of New York City's Drug Treatment Service Center, the city agency, said that just one high school in Ocean Hill Brownsville District had, quote, [[05:53:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21231.9s)]
*  Enough hardcore drug addicts to require the service resources of her entire agency. [[05:54:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21242.9s)]
*  And there were many, many schools like that. [[05:54:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21248.9s)]
*  Salzman wrote, quote, [[05:54:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21253.9s)]
*  Black students were angry about having to cope with subjects requiring the fundamental skills of reading, writing and arithmetic, with which they had never been provided in the earlier grades. [[05:54:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21272.9s)]
*  As a consequence, blacks experienced a sense of inferiority through having to compete with better trained white students in academic classes or being placed in the non-academic course of study for slow learners unable to do college preparatory work. [[05:54:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21283.9s)]
*  For more than four years prior to the disaster of 1969, the Lane staff had been witness to repeated acts of violence committed by black youngsters. [[05:54:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21297.9s)]
*  Teachers continually cried out against the growing lawlessness, but their pleas almost always fell on deaf ears. [[05:55:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21308.9s)]
*  In 1966, teachers who dared speak out against the deterioration of the school tone were labeled hysterical by the administration. [[05:55:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21315.9s)]
*  As the school fell apart in the mid-60s, so did its faculty. [[05:55:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21323.9s)]
*  Once a stable and tightly knit unit, the 1965 to 1969 period saw the most competent and experienced teachers find their way out of Lane, end quote. [[05:55:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21328.9s)]
*  In 1966, school officials wrote in a report to the city, [[05:55:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21341.9s)]
*  A dangerous and explosive atmosphere has existed at Lane High School since the opening of school in September. [[05:55:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21345.9s)]
*  There have been numerous cases of students being set upon, threatened and or beaten both on school grounds and in the immediate vicinity thereof. [[05:55:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21353.9s)]
*  The situation has deteriorated to the point where a teacher responsible for maintaining order in the student cafeteria was attacked, kicked in the stomach and sustained injuries requiring hospital treatment. [[05:56:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21362.9s)]
*  Many of these outbreaks have had racial overtones and have not been confined to boys alone, end quote. [[05:56:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21373.9s)]
*  The teachers at Lane were at a loss. [[05:56:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21381.9s)]
*  As Salzman said, a lot of the more experienced teachers, they left for greener pastures and so the teachers who were left behind and who were brought in were mostly inexperienced and they didn't know what to do. [[05:56:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21385.9s)]
*  So at an open school night, the teachers prepared a letter for the parents who attended that read in part, quote. [[05:56:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21397.9s)]
*  We know that your main reason for coming tonight is to find out how your child is progressing in his or her classes. [[05:56:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21406.9s)]
*  But we think that there is another matter you should know about, which may be even more important than homework and test marks. [[05:56:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21413.9s)]
*  And that has to do with the very safety of your child in the school building. [[05:56:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21419.9s)]
*  Nobody likes to admit that the problems of safety have gotten out of hand. [[05:57:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21423.9s)]
*  But the simple fact is that teachers alone cannot provide the kind of safety your child must have. [[05:57:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21428.9s)]
*  As parents, you have every right to expect that the school authorities will take all necessary steps to protect your child's person and property. [[05:57:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21434.9s)]

*  But Salzman refused and the principal threatened to bring charges against him and other union leaders. [[05:57:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21475.9s)]

*  Just before the beginning of one of his classes, Siracusa was preparing the classroom when a large rock crashed through the second storey. [[05:58:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21529.9s)]
*  The teacher inches up to the window, half expecting to be hit with another rock, and looks down and sees two black youths brazenly staring up at him. [[05:58:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21538.9s)]
*  Salzman says Siracusa was one of the more engaged teachers at the school and had spoken out recently against the increasing lawlessness at staff meetings, [[05:59:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21553.9s)]
*  a stance that drew the ire of black activists in the ATA and very likely led to his targeting. [[05:59:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21563.9s)]

*  Quote, Slowly he approached the two tall youngsters who were by now joined by a third youth, somewhat shorter and younger, but with as menacing of an ear as the older pair. [[05:59:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21579.9s)]

*  There was no reply, no discussion, not even a denial or an argument. [[06:00:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21600.9s)]
*  In a flash, one of the youngsters drew a water pistol from his jacket pocket, spraying the teacher's outer garments with a liquid that was later discovered to be highly flammable, lighter fluid. [[06:00:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21606.9s)]
*  Siracusa was befuddled. What's all this about? he thought to himself. [[06:00:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ga0tyBtGAds&t=21616.9s)]
